2013
Prof. Anantalal Thakur and Prof. Upendra Jha (eds.). Kāvyalakṣaṇa of Daṇḍin (also known as Kāvyādarśa) with Commentary Called Ratnaśrī of Ratnaśrījñāna. Darbhanga: Mithila Institute of Post-Graduate Studies and Research in Sanskrit Learning, 1957.

The printed edition that forms of the basis of this electronic edition is in the Devanāgarī script. The Devanāgarī version of this electronic edition was produced by double-keyboarding. The Romanized version was produced by automatic transliteration of the Devanāgarī version, using the standard IAST scheme of transliteration. Note that the printed edition is based on a single manuscript, and corrections to that manuscript are often made in the text rather than the apparatus. Some of the representational strategies of the printed edition (for example, printing a visarga within square brackets) are impossible to duplicate using the Unicode symbols for Devanāgarī (because they involve the independent use of characters that cannot be used independently), and hence they are followed with a /?/ in the Devanāgarī version. These problems do not arise in the Romanized version, but because this version has been generated automatically, the problem-marker /?/ still appears. Note also that the word-division of both the Romanized and Devanāgarī text is precisely as found in the source edition (i.e., yadyapi rather than yady api).

Daṇḍin's root-text is included in Ratnaśrījñāna's commentary. Daṇḍin's verses have the @type="mūla" (should one wish to extract them or display them separately or differently). I have organized the commentary into "blocks" (<div @type="sūtra">) that more or less correspond to sūtras of the root text, although sometimes Ratnaśrījñāna comments on several verses at a time. A special case are the extended treatments of particular figures, which are organized into "circles" (cakras); these are also contained in the same "block" elements (<div @type="sūtra">).

Cross-references have been tagged with standard abbreviations, based on the list found in Dwivedi's edition (2007) of the Śṛṅgāraprakāśa.

Third Pariccheda (Duṣkara)

[1] || śrīḥ || siṃhalācāryaratnaśrījñānakṛtayā ratnaśriyā ṭīkayā samalaṃkṛtam ācāryadaṇḍikṛtaṃ kāvyalakṣaṇam |
mārgavibhāgo nāma prathamaḥ paricchedaḥ |
caturmukhamukhāmbhojavanahaṃsavadhūrmama | mānase ramatāṃ nityaṃ sarvaśuklā sarasvatī || 1 ||

1* * * * * * * *

pūrvaśāstrāṇi saṃhṛtya prayogānupalakṣya ca | yathāsāmarthyamasmābhiḥ kriyate kāvyalakṣaṇam || 2 ||

* * * * * * * *

[2]
iha śiṣṭānuśiṣṭānāṃ śiṣṭānāmapi sarvathā | vācāmeva prasādena lokayātrā pravartate || 3 ||

* * * *

[ 4a ] doṣavibhāgato yathāvada ..........mallanāgo ........ vasthitilakṣaṇatvācca lokayātrāyā2 iti | viśiṣṭā lokayātrā [a]bhipretā na tu yā kācit | sā [vākśāstrarūpe]ti tadabhāve yathoktalokayātrānupapatteśca anyatrāpi yathāsambhavaṃ sāmānyaśabdāt viśeṣaḥ prasattavyaḥ | prasādena prabhāvānna..........| ataeva caturvargaśāsanāt śāstrā[ṇāṃ] caturvargavidyāśrayatvāt vidyāśrayasthānānīti ca nirucyate | tāni ca [śruti]smṛtyādīni saṃskṛtamayānītyāha [śiṣṭānuśiṣṭānāmiti | śiṣṭāḥ] [śabdā]nuśāsanakṛtaḥ pāṇiniprabhṛtayaḥ | tairanuśiṣṭāḥ saṃskṛtāḥ prakṛtipratyayādivibhāgakalpanayā 'nvā[khyātāḥ] tāsāṃ vācāṃ, śrutismūtyādīni hi catu[rvargasādhanāni] [saṃ]skṛtamayāni dṛśyante |

nanu bhāṣāntarairapi caturvargapratītilakṣaṇā lokayātrā pravartamānā dṛ[śyamānā]sti | tadapi śrutyādimūlamityatidiśannāha- śiṣṭā[nāma]pīti | śiṣṭānuśiṣṭebhyo bāhyāḥ śiṣṭāḥ pariśiṣṭāḥ | upayuktādanyaḥ śeṣa iti | tāsāṃ [pariśiṣṭānāṃ śāstravyavahāra]sthityā apabhraṃśasaṃgṛhītānām | yad vakṣyati—śāstreṣu saṃskṛtādanyadapabhraṃśatayoditam | iti | [1.36] evaṃ manyate...[i]damatra tāvat tātpa[ryam]........[lo]kayātrā śāstraprabhāvādeveti | tattu śāstraṃ saṃskṛtamayaṃ vā | bhāṣāntarasvabhāvaṃ prāyastu saṃskṛtamayaṃ dṛśyata iti | ata evāha- śi[ṣṭānuśiṣṭānāṃ.........evaṃ śāstrādeva sā | saṃskṛtetaralakṣaṇastu tadvikalpa eva | ataḥ sarvathā sarvaprakāreṇa ekāntena saṃskṛtādavaśiṣṭād vā śāstrādeva loka[yātrā pravartate |] kāvyaṃ cedaṃ caturvargalakṣaṇam | atrāpi guṇadoṣavivecane śāstraṃ śaraṇamityākūtam | vakṣyati ca—guṇadoṣānaśāstrajñaḥ [1.8] [3] ityādinā | yat punara[tra........kā]raṇamanyad vā yathā kathañcid ghuṇākṣaraprakhyaṃ dṛśyate tatrāpi śāstramastīti tadvidāṃ prayogapathānusārāt syāt | janmāntare vā kṛtaśāstrābhyā[saprati (4b) bu]ddhasaṃskārāṇāṃ pariniṣṭhitamapi syāt | yān sārasvatānanadhītapaṇḍitān vā vyavaharati lokaḥ | yadapi sarasvatīprasādāt kāvyakaraṇādikamiṣṭam, tadapi śāstrapra[bhāva]........prabhāvitatvāt | kiṃ bahunā ? sarvalokayātrā caturvargavyutpattilakṣaṇā śāstrādeva | tasmādidamapi kāvyaguṇadoṣavyutpattyarthaṃ karaṇīyameva, yataḥ parini[ṣṭhitaṃ kāvyaṃ jāya]ta iti bhāvaḥ ||

evamanvayeta lokayātrāṃ śāstramūlāṃ pratipādyaitadeva vyatirekeṇa draḍhayannāha—

idamandhaṃ tamaḥ kṛtsnaṃ jāyeta bhūvanatrayam | yadi śabdāhvayaṃ jyotirā saṃsārānna dīpyate || 4 ||

yadanantaramuktaṃ lokayā[trā]...........jyotirālokaḥ śabdāhvayaṃ śāstrasaṃjñakaṃ caturvargaprakāśakatvāt | śabda ityāhvayo yasyeti vigrahe, yadi na dīpyate na prakāśate na syādityarthaḥ | ke...........ro 'tra sattvalokaḥ | yaścaturvargamanutiṣṭhati tat maryādaṃ[?] ye tu muktāsteṣāṃ na saṃsārātmakatvam, nāpi caturvargānuṣṭhānam | sarva......[sva]rgamartyapātālalakṣaṇaṃ jagatrayaṃ sattvalokaḥ yasya caturvargapratipattiḥ sambhavati | idamiti | atya......tena vā tamo 'ndha[kāraḥ]........[la]kṣaṇalokayātrāvigamāt | apratipattikasaṃ[sārā]tmakaṃ syādityarthaḥ | kimekadeśena, netyāha- kṛts‍namiti | niravaśeṣaṃ nāṃśena tathāpya[lpam, netyā]ha- andhamiti | andhaṃ nirantarama[jñānatamoyogāt] caturvargapratipatteḥ kathañcidapyabhāvāt sarvathā nivṛttacaturvargajñānātmakaṃ jagat syāt | na ka[thañcid vastuprati]pattirbhavedityarthaḥ | yad vā, andhaṃtama.....[pṛ]ṣodarādidarśanāt siddham | arthastu sa eva | samādhiścaiṣa sarvathā 'jñāne nivṛtte sarvamatra gṛhyate [anva]yavyatirekābhyām | śāstrābhyāsaḥ kāvyaguṇadoṣavivekārthaṃ kriyata iti pūrvavadākūtam | ata evocyate—

śāstrādeva hi sarvatra guṇadoṣa[vicāra]ṇam | vinā śāstreṇa yat...................... ||

......ghaṭakaṃ śāstraviśeṣa eṣa vastutaḥ | tatrāpi caturvargapratipatteḥ | yad vakṣyati—caturvargaphalāyattami[tyādi] [1.15] [4] ......[5a] kāvyamiti vyavati[ṣṭhate]...........ityalaṃ vistareṇa ||

śāstrameva prakārāntareṇānusaṃharannāha—

ādirājayaśobimbamādarśaṃ prāpya vāḍmayam | teṣāmasannidhāne 'pi na svayaṃ paśya naśyati ||5 ||

ādayaḥ ādyāḥ pūrve rājānaḥ manvā[dyāḥ] teṣāmādirājānāṃ [guṇakhyāpakaṃ karma] yaśaskaratvād yaśa ityuktam | guṇā hi sākṣāt teṣāṃ śāstre kāvye vā varṇyante | guṇānāṃ tu prasiddhiḥ sarvalokakīrttanaṃ yaśaḥ | tadeva [śa]rīraṃ satpuruṣāṇāṃ........., śarīrapra[timatvāt | ta]duktam—

api svadehāt kimutendriyārthād yaśodhanānāṃ hi yaśo garīyaḥ | iti |
[raghuvaṃśe 14.35]

tadetat | vāgiha itihāsakathādilakṣaṇā, ādirā[jayaśaḥ]kīrttanāt | tatsvabhāvamādarśaṃ darpaṇam vaimalyāt, prāpya tatra pratibhāya tatpratyayārūḍhaṃ svayamātmanā na naśyati nāpagacchati yasyeti vismāpayannabhimukhayati param | ko 'tra vismaya i[ti cet ?] teṣāmasannidhāne 'pīti teṣāmādirājānāṃ yeṣāṃ tadbimbam | asannidhāne 'pi abhāve 'pi | idamatra citraṃ yat tadvato 'pagame 'pi bimbaṃ nāpaiti | darpaṇe hi tāvad bimbaṃ dṛśyate [yāvad vastusa]nnidhānam | apagate tu tadvati śarīre 'paiti | so 'yaṃ prasiddhādarśavilakṣaṇo 'pūrva eva kaścidādarśaḥ, yatrādirājalakṣaṇasya tadvato 'sannidhāvapi idānīm[api] bimbaṃ dṛśyate, na kevalaṃ sannidhāna ityapiśabdārthaḥ | atiśaye vā 'piśabdo vartate | asannidhāne 'pyaho dṛśyata ityatiśayaḥ | ata eva sarvā[tiśāyī] sanātanaḥ ko 'pyayamāloko lokayātrāpravṛttaye | kuto 'pyayamābhāti yaduta śāstraṃ nāmeti ||

śāstrād guṇadoṣaviveke sati ko guṇastad......āha—

gaurgauḥ kāmadughā samyakprayuktā smaryate budhaiḥ | duṣprayuktā punargotvaṃ prayoktaḥ saiva śaṃsati ||6 ||

gaurvāk kāvyādisvabhāvā | samyak śāstrādiprabhāveṇa svarūpato 'rthataśca pariśuddhā[5] prayuktā kṛtā prakāśitā satī puruṣeṇeti gamyate | kāma[dughā]......riti vakṣyamāṇamatrāpi sambandhanīyam | gauḥ saurabheyī smaryate ām‍nāyate budhairāptaiḥ | evamāptā upadiśanti, tasmādavitathametat | āptopadeśasya pramāṇatva[niścayāt][tadanusaraṇata]śceṣṭasiddhidarśanāt | yā vāgevaṃ kāmadhenurjātā suprayuktā satī saiva nānyā | duṣprayuktā punaḥ śāstravirodhāt svabhāvāśrayavaiguṇyenodbhāvitā tu sato gotvaṃ [paśutvaṃ śaṃ]sati khyāpayati prayoktuḥ puruṣasya | tataścāśāstrajño 'yaṃ puruṣākṛtiḥ paśuriti viduṣāṃ heyaḥ syādityanarthe patitaḥ | dūra evārthasiddhiḥ | tadiha ma[hada]ntaraṃ śāstra[jñānena bhavati | manuṣyatvā][5b]viśeṣe 'pi śāstrajño deva iva pūjyate guṇānurāgibhiritarastu paśuriva dṛśyata iti ||

yata evaṃ sarvatra guṇadoṣavivekaḥ śāstrādeva | guṇaśca puruṣārthena yojayati doṣaśca [itareṇa, ataḥ] śāstrānusāreṇa guṇavat [kāvyamekāntataḥ] puruṣārthasādhanam | doṣastu svalpo 'pi śāstraprabhāvādevāpaneyaḥ | anyathā heyaṃ syāditi prakṛtamanubadhnan āha—

tadalpamapi nopekṣyaṃ kāvyaṃ duṣṭaṃ kathañcana | syād vapuḥ sundaramapi śvitreṇaikena durbhagam || 7 ||

[duṣṭaṃ kāvyaṃ nope]kṣyaṃ kathañcanetyatrāpi yojyam | kenāpi prakāreṇa nopekṣaṇīyam | sarvathā 'paneyameva śāstradṛṣṭayā | anyathā heyaṃ syāt | tadeva prativastūpamayā sādhayannāhasyādityādi [vapuḥ śarīraṃ sundarama]pi varṇasaṃsthānasampannamapi prāgevāsundaram | ekena śvitreṇa kuṣṭhadoṣeṇa durbhagamaspṛśyaṃ heyaṃ syāt | sundaramapi śarīraṃ kuṣṭena svalpenāpyupa [pannaṃ heyaṃ yathā] tathā kaveḥ kāvyamayaṃ śarīraṃ śāśvataṃ sarvārthasādhanaṃ svalpenāpi śabdarūpeṇārthalakṣaṇena vā doṣeṇa śvitrakalpena pariharaṇīyaṃ syāt | prāgeva......ddhaṃ kāryaṃ karaṇīyam | doṣastu svalpo 'pi pariharaṇīyaḥ śāstradṛṣṭayeti |

kriyata eva nirdoṣaṃ kāvyaṃ vināpi śāstreṇetyāśaṅkya sarvaṃ śāstrādeva guṇadoṣa[parijñānaṃ kartavyami]ti pūrvoktakrameṇārthaṃ prativastūpamayā samarthayannāha—

guṇadoṣānaśāstrajñaḥ kathaṃ vibhajate janaḥ | kimandhasyādhikāro 'sti rūpabhedopalabdhiṣu || 8 ||

guṇā viśeṣā upādeyā arthāḥ puruṣārthasaṃgṛhītāstadviparītā doṣāḥ |......kāvyāpekṣayā tu śabdārthālaṅkārasvabhāvā guṇāḥ | doṣāstvapārthatvādayaḥ | śleṣaviparyāsādayaśca[6] vaidarbhamārgāpekṣayā vakṣyamāṇāḥ | ata eva sāmānyenāha—guṇadoṣānaśāstrajñaḥ kathaṃ vibhajate janaḥiti | sarvamapi sā[mānyaṃ e]kasyāpyarthasya prakṛtāpekṣayā viśeṣaniṣṭhaṃ bhaviṣyatīti nipuṇeyaṃ vācoyuktiḥ | tān guṇadoṣān yo na vetti puruṣaḥ[sa] kathaṃ vibhajate [vibhaktānkaro]ti ete guṇāḥ [ete doṣā i]ti | ya[to guṇānāda]tte doṣāna hāsyati kathañcit | kiṃ na vibhajate, aśāstrajño yataḥ | śāstrādeva hi guṇadoṣā vivecyante | yaśca śāstraṃ guṇadoṣaviveka[viṣa][6a]yaṃ na vetti, kathaṃ tasyāpratipannopāyasya guṇadoṣavivekalakṣaṇamupeyaṃ setsyati | yathā tvasya rūpava......................kimandhasyetyādi | andhasya cakṣurvikalasya rūpabhedānāṃ nīlapītādīnāṃ rūpaviśeṣāṇāṃ upa[la]bdhiṣu darśane[ṣu nādhiṃkāraḥ | i ]ha sāmānyena rūpaṃ nāma kiñcidastīti śrutimātrakamapaśyataḥ syāt | na tu rūpaviśeṣasākṣātkā[raḥ | viśeṣajñānābhāve] na ca tat kvacidupayujyate | tato yadāhamanuṣṭhānā[?]bhāvād vibhāgena tu sarvātmanā śāstra......[vibha]jata ityāha | tadevamiyatā granthena śāstrādeva sarvaguṇadoṣavivekato nānyathā kāvye 'pi......

ataḥ prajānāṃ vyutpattimabhisandhāya sūrayaḥ | vācāṃ vicitramārgāṇāṃ nibabandhuḥ kriyāvidhim || 9 ||

ataḥ kāraṇāt sūrayaḥ pūrvācāryāḥ kriyāvidhiṃ nibabandhuriti saṃbandha | kriyāvidhiṃ kriyākalpam.........[malla]nāgena3 vidyāsamuddeśe kriyākalpa iti kāvyālaṅkāra uktaḥ | tadanusāreṇānena kriyākalpaḥ kriyā .........[vidhī]yate 'neneti kriyāvidhiḥ | kriyākalpo 'pi evamiti nārthataḥ kaścid bhedaḥ | kāvyalakṣaṇaṃ śāstraṃ kṛtavantaḥ | [śāstrānusāreṇa mūrkho] 'pi pravartate | kiṃ punarbuddhimān lokaḥ | tasmāt sarvatra nmatamiti | vyutpattimabhisandhāya kāvye yathāvad guṇadoṣaparijñāna[hetubhiḥ śāstra]saṃgṛhītairguṇadoṣaviveko vyutpattiḥ tadupādānahāniphalā 'bhidheyā | catuvarga iti ca nānāprakāraḥ sarvapuruṣārthaḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ | asyaiva tu [śāstrasya prameyaśca]turvargaḥ | tatpratipādakaṃ śāstraṃ tādarthyāt | etāvāneva ca puruṣārthaḥ | tatra sarvatra guṇāśca doṣāśca jñātavyāḥ | tatra guṇā vastutaḥ puruṣārthamayā eva | tatasta upāde[yāḥ] upādeyatayā [ca]jñeyāstathārthenājñātānāmupādānāsambhavāt | doṣāstu tadābhāsāstatsaṃbhavino heyāḥ | te 'pi heyatayā jñeyāstathā bhāvenājñātānāṃ hānāsaṃbhavāt | [6b] [vi]vekaśca samyak [7] śāstrādeva dṛṣṭārthādadṛṣṭārthād veti sarvaśāstrasthitireṣā | kāvyamapyetat trividhaṃ catu rvargarūpaṃ caturvargastadupāyaścānena rasāntaraparigraheṇa pratipādya[pratipā]dakatvāt | śabdātmakamapi kāvyaśarīraṃ caturvargastādarthyāt | upāyo 'pi tādarthyāccaturvargaḥ |

mukhyastāvaccaturvargaḥ pumarthāśeṣasaṃgrahaḥ | tadupāye 'pi tādarthyācchāstreṣvapi [samādaraḥ] ||

iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ |

kiṃ ca kāvyeneṣṭadevatāviṣayavicitrastotralakṣaṇena samyag‌viracitena dharmo 'prameyaḥ | tathātve ca kadācid varalābhādiko 'rthaḥ | sukha[m]pyetatpuruṣārtha[dvaya]niṣṭhamuktam |

buddhastotragranthanavyāpṛtānāṃ bhaktiprahveṣvindriyeṣu dravatsu | ekaikasmin yaḥ kṣaṇe puṇyakośo nāsarvajñastaṃ pramātuṃ samarthaḥ || iti |

guṇajñarājādi[varṇanātoḥpyaryāti]śayaprāptistadarthācca dharmaḥ sukhaṃ ca sampatsyete | kiṃ bahunā, na so 'sti puruṣārthaḥ kaścid yaḥ kāvyāt parigṛhītāśrayaviśeṣā[nna jāyate | i]hānuṣaṅge guṇadoṣavibhāgaḥ karaṇīyaḥ | sa ca śāstrādeva nānyatheti vistareṇa pūrvameva pratipāditam | tataḥ kā[vyakriyā]vidhimiti prakṛtam | kasya vyutpattimabhisandhāyetyāha-prajānāmiti | lokasya santāne kā vyutpattiḥ kathaṃ [keṣāṃ ?] nāma...... [vyutpādanakri]yāmabhisandhāya kriyāvidhiṃ nibabandhurityāha-vācāṃ vicitramārgāṇāmiti | vicitro nānāprakāraḥ śabdālaṃkārā[rthālaṃkārādiyukto mārgaḥ] kāvyānyeva | tataḥ kāvyaviṣayāṃ lokakartṛkāṃ kāvyaguṇadoṣavibhāgavijñānalakṣaṇāṃ vyutpattimuddiśya [śāstranirmāṇam] | tatsaṃkṣepatvād idamapi saprayojanamiti karttavyameva | tataśca sāmānyena kāvyalakṣaṇaśāstrāj‌jñeya iyatā viśiṣyocyate ||

[kāvyala]kṣaṇamidānīṃ kartumārabhate—

taiḥ śarīraṃ ca kāvyānāmalaṅkāraśca darśitaḥ | śarīraṃ tāvadiṣṭārthavyavacchinnā padāvalī || 10 ||

iha yoni kānicit kāvyāni saṃbhavanti teṣāṃ [śarīramalaṅkāraśca] taiḥ pūrvācāryaiḥ lokasya kāvyavyutpattaye kriyākalpe nibaddhe | tayoḥ kīdṛśaṃ śarīram [śabdarūpam | arthe][7a]nāviṣṭatvāt | yathā hi puruṣaśarīre hārakeyūrādiralaṃkāro nyasyate yena[8] śobhate, tathā kāvyaśarīre [śabdamaye 'pyupamādirarpya]te, yataḥ śobhā | [va]kṣyate [ca]—kāvyaśobhākarān dharmānalaṃkārān pracakṣate || iti | [2.1] paścādalaṅkāro vakṣyate | padānāṃ subantati[ṅantānāṃ āvalī śreṇī, tayā] paripūrṇaṃ kāvyaṃ [tasya] ślokādayo 'vayavā avāntaravākyāni | kavinā vaktumiṣṭe 'bhiprete 'rthe kasmiṃścid raghuvaṃśādau | vyavacchinnā gamakatve[na]...svīkṛtā | viśeṣe[ṇa]... ......[śarī]raṃ vijñeyamitīṣṭārthavyavacchinnā padāvalī prasiddhatvādanūdyāprasiddhaṃ śarīraṃ vidhīyate | yathā yaḥ.............

[śa]rīraṃ katividhamityāha—

padyaṃ gadyaṃ ca miśraṃ ca tat tridhaiva vyavasthitam | padyaṃ catuṣpadī tacca vṛttaṃ jātiriti dvidhā || 11 ||

yadanantaraṃ lakṣaṇataḥ kathitaṃ taccharīraṃ prabhedataḥ tridhaiva triprakārameva vyavasthitaṃ boddhavyam |.........[ke]valapadyātmakaṃ......[kevalagadyātmakaṃ gadyapadyobhayātmakaṃ ca]... ityanekena prakāreṇa tridhaiva vyavasthitamiti prakṛtam | tatra padyaṃ na jñāyate kiṃrūpamityata āha-padyaṃ catuṣpadītyādi |.........anūdya padyamiti jñā[payati catuṣpadī] tat padyaṃ jñeyamiti | tacca padyaṃ dvidhā dviprabhedamavaseyam | katham—vṛttaṃ jātirityanena rūpeṇa ||

tadapi na jñāyate kiṃ vṛttaṃ jāti[rvā kīdṛśī]ti | tadāha—

chandovicityāṃ sakalastatprapañco nidarśitaḥ | sā vidyā naurvivikṣūṇāṃ gambhīraṃ kāvyasāgaram || 12 ||

tayorvṛttajā[tyoḥ prapañco] vicitraḥ prabhedaḥ vaktrādirūpaḥ, āryādilakṣaṇaśca sakalaḥ sarvo nidarśitaḥ lakṣaṇato lakṣitaśca pratipāditaḥ | kutra chando[vicityāṃ chandāṃsi] vicīyante [saṃgṛhyante yatra] yayā vā tasyām | sā ceyaṃ vidyā padyalakṣaṇasya kāvyaśarīrasya sādhikā | yadana[yā] prasādhyate tataḥ sāpyādareṇa draṣṭavyeti vakroktyā tadabhyāse śrotṛjanaṃ niyoja[yati- sā vidyeti] kāvyame[va sāgaraḥ tadvad]gambhīraṃ yataḥ, [9] bhāvārthagāmbhīryāt | na tu śabdagāmbhīryeṇa | anyathā pramādo na syāt | nānārasāmṛtatvāt | sūktaratnākaratvāt | akṛtadhiyāṃ ca [vairasyādhāyakatvāt] kāvyasāgaraṃ vi[vikṣūṇāṃ avagā]hitumicchatāṃ svayaṃ kartuṃ parakīyaṃ vā jñātumicchatāmityarthaḥ | sā chandovicitividyā naurūpā | sāpi jñātavyeti bhāvaḥ ||

saṃghātādyapi vṛttajātiprakāro 'sti chandaḥśāstroktaḥ [7b] [sa i]ha kiṃ na darśita iti cet, āha—

muktakaṃ kulakaṃ kośaḥ saṃghāta iti tādṛśaḥ | sargabandhāṃśarūpatvādanuktaḥ padyavistaraḥ || 13 ||

ekaḥ ślokaḥ samāptārthaḥ svatantraḥ ślokāntaranirapekṣa iti muktakam, na tu nibaddhamiti sargabandhena [vaiṣamyaṃ] bandhe 'nibandhanāt | yad vakṣyati—sargabandhāṃśarūpatvāt [1.13] iti |

ekakriyādvāreṇa parasparasāpekṣāḥ samāptārthāḥ pratyekamasamāptārthāḥ ślokāḥ kulakam | tadviśeṣa eva yugalakam | nānābhittayo bhinnakriyāḥ svatantrāḥ ślokāḥ kośavat sthā[pitāḥ kośaḥ] | ekāṃ bhittiṃ prāvṛḍādikāṃ varṇayituṃ samudāyena pravṛttā bhinnakriyāḥ ślokāḥ saṃghātaḥ | iti tādṛśaḥ | ityevaṃrūpaścaturvidhapadyaprakāro 'nukto [viśiṣya] pṛthagiha la[kṣaṇataḥ anuktaḥ akathita]styakta eva | kiṃ kāraṇam | sargabandhāṃśarūpatvāt sargabandhasya aṃśarūpā, ekadeśasvabhāvāsteṣāṃ bhāvastattvam | tasmāt te hi saṃ[gṛhītāḥ | na] muktatā[divyati]rekeṇa sargabandhaḥ se[tsya]ti, tantuvyatirekeṇa paṭavat | sa ca lakṣaṇata ucyata eva | tataste 'pi tadavyatirekā[t] pṛthagasargaba[ndharūpa]to noktā ityarthaḥ |

nanvevaṃ stotrāvadānaparikathādipadyaprapañco na saṃgṛhītaḥ syāt | saṃgṛhīta eva | [ukta]lakṣaṇayogāt......[saṃ]ghātaḥ āryā kośa iti saṃghātādisaṃjñāpravṛttimātreṇa saṃghātāditvaṃ sargabandhāṃśasya saṃghātāderata[stad‌rūpa]tvaṃ stotrādīnāṃ...... | nahi sargabandhasya śiśupālavadhādināmāntarakaraṇamātreṇa sargabandhatvaṃ hīyate | tasmāt sttotrādirapi lakṣaṇa[taḥ saṃghā]tādisaṃgṛhītaḥ ...nahi karkādivyapadeśāntarayogādaśvatvaṃ hīyate, aśvaviśeṣāḥ karkādaya iti cet-stotrādayo 'pi yathālakṣa[ṇaṃ]......nimittaṃ(?) yathe[ha sarga]bandhe ca saṃghātādiḥ parimphuṭaṃ lakṣyata eva | tatra hi prāvṛḍvarṇanādiḥ[10] saṃghātaḥ | mantrādyavasare ca yathā[muktakādistatho]ktaṃ prāk | muktakaṃ......[itya8a]tra parisphuṭamevetyalaṃ vistareṇa ||

kaḥ punaḥ sargabandho yasyāvathavāḥ saṃghātādaya ityāha—

sargabandho mahākāvyamucyate tvasya lakṣaṇam | āśīrnamaskriyā vastunirdeśo vāpi tanmukham || 14 ||

yadetat prasiddhaṃ guṇataḥ sanniveśataśca mahākāvyamiti sargabandhaḥ...[sa]...vijñaya iti mahākāvyānuvādena sargabandho vidhīyate | sargaiḥ sargākhyaiḥ paricchedaviśeṣairbadhyate 'sāviti sargabandhaḥ | tataścānekasargātmakaḥ sargabandho mahākāvyam | sargāśca saṃghātādicatuṣṭyasvabhāvā iti draṣṭavyam |

athavā anyathāvatāryate | nanu muktakādayo mahākāvyasyāṃśāḥ, tat kimucyate—sargabandhāṃśarūpatvāt [1.13] ityāha—sargabandho mahākāvyamiti | sargabandha ityapi mahākāvyamucyate | tato ye [ma]hākāvyasyāṃśāste sargabandhasyāpītyavirodha ityarthaḥ | śeṣaṃ samānam |

sargabandhasya tarhi kiṃ lakṣaṇaṃ yat tadaṃśasya saṃghātāderapi syādityāha—ucyate tvasya lakṣaṇam | tuśabdo bhinnakramaḥ | asya tu mahākāvyasya lakṣaṇaṃ svarūpamucyate | tuśabdenaitadāha-saṃghātādīnāmavayavānāṃ pṛthag lakṣaṇaṃ nocyate | avayavinastu mahākāvyasya lakṣaṇaṃ kriyate | tataste 'pi tallakṣaṇā eva, vastutastadavyatirekāditi | kiṃ punastaditi tadeva vaktumupakramate-āśīrityādi | tasya mahākāvyasya mukhamādiḥ āśīriṣṭāśaṃsanaṃ vā prayujyate, namaskriyā praṇāmo vā, prabandhasambandhinaḥ kasyacid vastuno 'rthasya nirdeśaḥ kathanaṃ vā kriyate iti vikalpena trividhaṃ mukhaṃ pratipattavyam | na samuccayena | tatra

śrīmadviśuddhaguṇarat‍nanasa[mi]ddhamūrtti- rbrahmendraśekharitapādasarojareṇuḥ | [11] śauddhodaniḥ sakalasattvahitaikadīkṣaḥ pāyādapāyabahulājjagadāvimukteḥ ||

ityevaṃvidhā āśīḥ |

namastrayāya rat‍nānāṃ trailokya[mahitā]tmane | sthitāya suratadvairinaranāgendramauliṣu ||

ityevaṃvidhā namaskriyā | vastunirdeśastu śriyaḥ patiḥ śrīmati [śiśupālavadhe 1.1] ityādiḥ prasiddha eva |

gadyamiśrabandhayorapyetadeva mukhaṃ draṣṭavyamiti ||

kimāśrayaṃ tadityāha—

itihāsakathodbhūtamitaradvā sadāśrayam | catuvargaphalāyattaṃ caturodāttanāyakam || 15 ||

itihāsaḥ purāvṛttam, tatpratipādikā kathā rāmāyaṇādikā itihāsakathā tata udbhūtaṃ jātam, itihāsakathāśrayamityarthaḥ | kā[vyami]ti vakṣyati | kimitihāsakathāśrayameva mahākāvyaṃ kartavyam | netyāha-itaraditi | itihāsakathāśrayādaparaṃ vā | nātra niyamaḥ, viśiṣṭāśrayameva tu tat kartavyamiti- sadāśrayamiti | san śobhanaḥ adhiguṇarājacaritādilakṣaṇā āśrayo bhittiryasya tattathā | anena mahākāvyasya dvidhāśrayasampaduktā |

caturviṣayatvaṃ pratipādayannāha—caturvargaphalāyattam caturṇāṃ dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ vargaḥ samūhaḥ, sa eva phalaṃ puruṣārthatpatvāt | tatrā 'bhyudayaniḥśreyasaheturdharma4 | vidyābhūmyādīnāṃ yathānyāyamarjanamarjitānāṃ ca rakṣaṇamarthaḥ | nirapāyo viṣayopabhogaḥ kāmaḥ | [traikālika]sāṃsārikaduḥkhanivṛttirmokṣaḥ | vistarastu ta[tta]cchāstrebhyo draṣṭavyaḥ | tasminnāyattaṃ pratibaddhaṃ tadviṣayatvāt | atra na niyamo 'vaśyaṃ catvāro 'pi puruṣārthā nibadhyanta iti | yathāsaṃbhavaṃ kvaciccaturvargaḥ, [kvaci]t trivarga iti [12] pratipattavyam | etacca svayameva vakṣyati—nyūnamapyatra yaiḥ kaiścit [1.20] ityādau | caturodāttanāyakam | caturaḥ kuśalaḥ utyāhaśaktyādiyogāt | udātta udārastyāgātiśayādisaṃbandhāt nāyakaḥ vipakṣaḥ pratipakṣaśca5 | dvayorapi nāyakatvāt, yasmin tat tathā ||

punaḥ kiṃ viśiṣṭamityāha—

nagarārṇavaśailartucandrārkodayavarṇanaiḥ | udyānasalilakrīḍāmadhupānaratotsavaiḥ || 16 ||

candraścārkaśca tayorudayaḥ | nagaraṃ ca arṇavaśca śailaśca ṛtuśca candrārkodayaśceti cārthaṃ kṛtvā teṣāṃ varṇanāni guṇodbhāvanāni iti ṣaṣṭhīsamāsaḥ | tāni ca yathāsambhavamādau madhye 'nte vā | na cānukramaniya[mena] etāni nibadhyanta iti evaṃparametat | tairalaṃkṛtamiti [1.18] vakṣyati | udyānaṃ salilaṃ ca tayoḥ krīḍā vihāraḥ | sā ca madhupānakaṃ ca ratotsavaśceti cārthaḥ | ratamevotsavaḥ prītiviśeṣaḥ, teṣāṃ tu kramo dṛśyate | anena sambhogātmakaḥ śrṛṅgāra uktaḥ | tairalaṃkṛtam ||

punarviśeṣayannāha—

vipralambhairvivāhaiśca kumārodayavarṇanaiḥ | mantradūtaprayāṇājināyakābhyudayairapi || 17 ||

vipralambhā virahāḥ | ayaṃ vipralambhātmakaḥ śrṛṅgāraḥ | vivāhāḥ śāstroktā gandharvādayaḥ | kumārāṇāmudayā janmāni vadhanāni ca bālyādivayaḥprāptilakṣaṇāni | taiścālaṃkṛtam | mantraḥ kriyārambhadeśakālavibhāgapuruṣadravyasamyag‌vinipātakriyākāryasiddhilakṣaṇapañcāṅgātmakakāryaniścayaḥ | yadāha māghaḥ—

sarvakāryaśarīreṣu muktvāṅgaskandhapañcakam | saugatānāmivātmānyo nāsti mantro mahībhṛtām |
[śiśupālavadhe 2.28] [13] iti | vistarastu tacchāstrāt | dūtaḥ vāgmitvādiguṇayuktaḥ sandhānapravṛttaḥ puruṣaḥ | dūte sandhānamāyattaṃ care caryā prati[tī]ṣṭhatā | [kāmandakīyanītisāre 12.33] iti vacanāt | caraviśeṣaścāyam | prayāṇaṃ saṃgrāmādinimittaṃ gamanam | ājiviṃgrahaḥ sandhyabhāve | abhyudayaṃ vipakṣavijayādilakṣaṇa utsavaḥ | nāyakasya pratipakṣasya | eṣāma[pyā]nupūrvī dṛśyate | tairapi |

alaṃkṛtamasaṃkṣiptarasabhāvanirantaram | sargairanativistīrṇaiḥ śravyavṛttaiḥ susandhibhiḥ || 18 ||

alaṃkṛtaṃ vibhūṣitam | asaṃkṣiptāḥ [9a]bhūyāṃsaḥ | rasāḥ śrṛṅgāravīrādayaḥ | bhāvā ratyutsavādayaḥ | vistarastu tacchāstrāt | tairnirantaraṃ vyāptam | sargairupetamiti [1.19] vakṣyati | anativistīrṇairnātimahadbhirmadhyamairityarthaḥ | śravyaṃ śruti[su]bhagaṃ vṛttaṃ padyamindravajrādikaṃ yeṣāṃ taiḥ | susandhibhiḥ śobhanaḥ spaṣṭaḥ sandhiḥ parasparasaṅgatatvam anyo 'nyavyapekṣā arthato yeṣāṃ taiḥ | parasparasaṃbaddhārthāḥ sargāḥ kartavyāḥ | natvayaḥśalākākalpā ityarthaḥ ||

sarvatra bhinnavṛttāntairupetaṃ lokarañjanam | kāvyaṃ kalpāntarasthāyi jāyate sadalaṃkṛti || 19 ||

bhinnaḥ prakṛtavṛttāpekṣayā anyavṛttalakṣaṇaḥ sargāṇāmanto 'vasānaṃ yeṣām | kiṃ kvacideva sarge netyāha-sarveṣu sargeṣu | sargāḥ prastutapadyāpekṣayā vṛttāntaraiḥ samāpanīyā ityarthaḥ | tai revaṃrūpaiḥ sargairupetaṃ yuktam | sadalaṃkṛti satyaḥ śobhanāḥ suprayuktatvāt | natvalaṃkṛtayaḥ svarūpeṇa śobhanā nāma | alaṃkṛtayaḥ śabdārthālaṃkārāḥ yasya yasmin vā tat tathā | satyo vā vidyamānā alaṃkṛtayo yasya tadevaṃvidhaṃ kāvyaṃ lokarañjanaṃ jāyate | lokaṃ rañjayati guṇasaṃpadā paritoṣayati iti lokarañjanam | tataśca pratigrāhakabhūyastvāt kalpāntaraṃ tiṣṭhantīti kalpāntarasthāyi.........[jā]yate bhavati pravacanavat yāvajjagat pravartata ityarthaḥ ||

nanu sarvatra mahākāvye caturvargādīnyaṅgāni yathoktāni na dṛśyante | kānicideva kvacid [dṛśyante] | tanna kiñcididānīṃ mahākāvyaṃ syādityāha—

[14]
nyūnamapyatra yaiḥ kaiścidaṅgeḥ kāvyaṃ na varjyate | yadyupātteṣu sampattirārādhayati tadvidaḥ || 20 ||

atrokteṣvaṅgeṣu avayaveṣu yaiḥ kaiścid yathāsambhavaṃ tu madhupānakumārodayaparvatavarṇanādibhirnyūnaṃ rahita[ma]pi, na ke[va]laṃ pūrṇaṃ kāvyaṃ, mahākāvyaṃ na varjyate sadbhirupādīyata ityarthaḥ | na duṣyatītyapi pāṭhaḥ | astu sa eva | asyotsargasyāpavādamāhayadītyādi | upātteṣu [gṛhīte]ṣu sampattirvibhūtiḥ śabdārthasādguṇyalakṣaṇā | tadvidaḥ tāṃ kāvyasampattiṃ ye vidanti tān puruṣān ārādhayati rañjayati yadi, tadā navarjyate | arthopāttānyaṅgāni | yad vi[gatārthaṃ] tad heyamityarthād gamyate |

atredaṃ cintyate | kathamatra kramaḥ | kiṃ pūrvavarṇitena nāyakena riporjayāt nāyakasyotkarṣaḥ kathyate | atha prāg‌varṇi[tasya ri]pornāyakena jayāt tadutkarṣaḥ khyāpyata iti | atra bhāmahaḥ pūrvakameva kramamicchati, dvitīyaṃ tu dveṣṭi—

nāyakaṃ prāgupanyasya vaṃśavīryaśrutādibhiḥ | na tasyaiva vadhaṃ kuryādanyotkarṣābhidhitsayā ||
yadi kāvyaśarīrasya na sa vyāpitayeṣyate | na cābhyudayabhāk tasya mudhā ' 'dau grahaṇaṃ stave ||
[kāvyālaṅkāre 1.22-23]

iti | daṇḍī tu prakāradvayamapi yuktamicchannāha—

guṇataḥ prāgupanyasya nāyakaṃ tena vidviṣām | nirākaraṇamityeṣa mārgaḥ prakṛtisundaraḥ || 21 ||

nā[yakaṃ prati]pakṣaṃ prāk prathamamupanyasyābhidhāya guṇato guṇaiḥ śauryādibhirabhilakṣitaṃ nāyakaṃ pūrva varṇayitvetyarthaḥ | tena pūrvavarṇitena nāyakena vidviṣāṃ vipakṣāṇāṃ nirākaraṇamabhibha[vaḥ parāja]yaḥ kathyata iti eṣa mārgaḥ kramaḥ prakṛtyā sundaraḥ śobhanaḥ | svarūpasiddha ṛjurayaṃ krama iti manyate ||

dvitīyaṃ kramamāha, yo bhāmahena dviṣṭaḥ—

vaṃśavīryaśrutādīni varṇayitvā riporapi | tajjayānnāyakotkarṣakathanaṃ ca dhinoti naḥ || 22 ||
[15]

ripo[rnāyakavi]pakṣasyāpi na kevalaṃ pratipakṣasya vaṃśo 'nvayaḥ vīrya vikramaḥ śrataṃ śāstrakauśalaṃ ādiryeṣāṃ tyāgasatyakṣāntyādīnāṃ tāni guṇavastūni varṇayitvā prakāśya [tasya] varṇitavaṃśādervipakṣasya jayād abhibhavāt kāraṇāt pratipakṣeṇa, nāyakasya pratipakṣasya utkarṣo viśeṣaḥ tasya kathanamabhidhānaṃ yat, tacca no 'smān dhinoti prīṇyati | cakārāt pūrvakaṃ ca | ayamapi kramo 'smākaṃ priya evetyarthaḥ |

ayamabhiprāyaḥ—kāvyaṃ hi vakroktipradhānam | ayaṃ ca kramaḥ vakroktisvabhāvaḥ, yadvipakṣavarṇanadvāreṇa pratipakṣotkarṣakathanam | evaṃ nāmāyamuktṛṣṭaḥ, yadevaṃguṇo 'pi vipakṣo[ 'nena] nirjita iti | anyaśca varṇito 'nyasyotkarṣaḥ khyāpyata iti caturo 'yaṃ [na]yaḥ |tasmādayamasmān dhinotīti | kāvyeṣu hi dvāvapi varṇyete kevalaṃ paurvāparyayorvivādaḥ | atra hi pratipakṣotkarṣo vidheyaḥ | sa cobhayathā 'pi gamyata eva | hayagrīvavadhādau cāyaṃ [pra][10a]kāro dṛśyate ṛjunaiva krameṇa | pratipakṣotkarṣaḥ kiṃ na kathyate vakroktyā kiṃ na khyāpyate vakrīktipradhānatvāt kāvyasyeti cet | yatkiñcidetat | 6aśokavanikācodyamidam |

yaducyate kāvyaśarīrāvyāpakatvāt, anabhyudayabhāgitvācca vipakṣasya prāgunyāsavarṇane viphala iti | tadasat | kathaṃ pratipakṣotkarṣakhyāpanaparaṃ vipakṣavarṇanaṃ prākkriyamāṇaṃ viphalaṃ nā[ma] | evaṃ hi prākpratipakṣanāyakavarṇanam, tena ca vipakṣanāyakanirākaraṇamitīdamapi pratipakṣotkarṣārthaṃ kriyamāṇaṃ viphalaṃ syāt | atha pratipakṣotkarṣakathanārthatvāt nanu7 caitat pratipa[kṣa]varṇanamapi pratipakṣotkarṣakhyāpanārthatvāt na mugheti na kaścid viśeṣo 'nyatrābhiniveśāt | tasmāt kāvyaśarīrāvyāptyanabhyudayabhāgino 'pi vipakṣasya prāk graha[ṇa]stavau na mudhaiva, pratipakṣotkarṣakhyāpanārthatvāt, pratipakṣavarṇanādivaditi dvayamapi sādhu dṛśyatāmiti ||

yat pūrvaṃ kāvyaśarīraṃ trividhoddiṣṭaṃ padyaṃ gadyaṃ ca miśraṃ ceti [1.11] tatraitā[vatā] padyaṃ nirdiṣṭam | gadyamadhikṛtyāha—

apādaḥ padasaṃtāno gadyamākhyāyikā kathā | iti tasya prabhedau dvau

na vidyate pādaḥ pādavyavasthā yasminniti na pādo vā apādaḥ pādasvabhāvo na bhavatī-[16]tyarthaḥ | evalakṣaṇaṃ gadyam | padyaṃ tu pādasvabhāvaḥ padasantāna ityasaṅkaraḥ | katividhaṃ tadityāha—ākhyāyiketyādi | tasya gadyasya bhedau prakārau dvau vijñeyau | katham | ākhyāyikākathetyevaṃ[rū]pau | [na] anayorbhedaḥ | bhāmahamatena bhedamāha—

tayorākhyāyikā kila || 23 ||
nāyakenaiva vācyānyā nāyakenetareṇa vā | svaguṇāviṣkriyādoṣo nātra bhūtārthaśaṃsataḥ || 24 ||

tayorākhyāyikākathayorayaṃ bhedaḥ kileti paramatasūcane | ākhyāyikā nāyakenaiva [svayam][10b] ucyate, yasya caritapratipādanārthamākhyāyikā pravṛttā | nānyeneti vaktṛniyamaḥ ākhyāyikāyām | taduktam—vṛttamākhyāyate yasyāṃ nāyakena svaceṣṭitam | iti | [kāvyālaṅkāre 1. 26]

anyā kathā uktāyā ākhyāyikāyā anyatvāt | nāyakena vācyā yaccaritaprakāśanāya pravṛttā, itareṇa vā nāyakādanyena vā, tatsahāyādinā vācyeti na vaktṛniyamaḥ kathāyām | ayaṃ tāvadanayorbhedaḥ |

na[nviya]mākhyāyikā svayaṃ nāyakenocyate na kathā | evaṃ hi svaguṇodbhāvanaprasaṅgaḥ | taccānucitamabhijātasya | taduktam-svaguṇāviṣkṛtiṃ kuryādabhijātaḥ kathaṃ janaḥ | iti | [kāvyālaṅkāre 1.29]

atrāha—svaguṇāviṣkriyetyādi | ayaṃ tāvadadoṣaḥ | yataḥ svasyātmanaḥ sveṣāṃ vā guṇānāṃ vaṃśasya vīryādīnāmāviṣkriyā prastāvavaśāt kathanaṃ na doṣaḥ na duṣyati | kasya—bhūtaṃ yathāvṛttamarthaṃ svacā[ritrya]lakṣaṇaṃ śaṃsato bruvato nāyakasya | atrākhyāyikāyāṃ kathāyāṃ vā | tena hi yathāvṛttaṃ svacaritamamidheyaṃ doṣarūpaṃ guṇarūpamanyadvā, na viparītam | tat[a]viparītaṃ yathāvṛttamātmanaḥ kathayataḥ prastāvavaśaprāptaṃ svaguṇakathanaṃ kathamābhijātyaṃ hāpayet | pratyuta viparītāmidhāne ābhijātyaṃ hīyeta | ātmava[ñcana]rūpaṃ tu svaguṇāviṣkaraṇamanucitamābhijātye |

[17]

nanu nātra doṣa ityetāvaduktam | guṇastu na kaścit | ayameva guṇo yo doṣābhāvaḥ | tallakṣaṇatvāttasya sarvatreti yat‌tkiñcidetam | a[nena] caitannirastaṃ bhaṅgayā yaduktaṃ bhāmahena, ākhyāyikāyāṃ sukhaduḥkharūpaṃ svacaritaṃ yathāvṛttamākhyāyate nāyakena na tu guṇarūpamiti | vṛttamākhyāyate yasyāṃ nāyakena svaceṣṭa[11a]nāditi |

nanu sāmānyavacanametat | na tvayaṃ viśeṣo dṛśyate duḥkharūpaṃ svacaritaṃ vācyaṃ na guṇarūpamiti | arthādetaduktaṃ tena | yatpaścāt vakṣyati—svaguṇāviṣkṛtiṃ kuryādabhijātaḥ [kāvyālaṅkāre 1.29] iti | anyathā pūrvāparavirodhastatra syāt ||

kiṃ tarhi na yuktamiti svamatamāha—

api tvaniyamo dṛṣṭastatrāpyanyairudīraṇāt | anyo vaktā svayaṃ veti kīdṛg vā bhedakāraṇam || 25 ||

kiṃ tvidamatra brūmaḥ | yaḥ pareṇa niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ ākhyāyikā nāyakenaiva vācyeti, sa nāsti | yatastatrākhyāyikāyāmapi na kevalaṃ kathāyām, aniyamaḥ nāyakenaiva vācyetyasya niyamasyābhāvo dṛṣṭaḥ upalabdhaḥ kṛtaḥ | anyairudīraṇāt nāyakādanyairapi tadanucarādibhirākhyāyikāyā udīraṇāt vacanāt | harṣacaritādikāyāmākhyāyikāyāmanyairapi nāyakacaritakathanadarśanāditi manyate | sarvathā kaviriha vaktā, tanmukhena nāyako vā, svātantryamatra kaveḥ | nanu bhāmahena kathāyāḥ parodīraṇamiṣṭaṃ, yadāha—anyaiḥ svacaritaṃ tasya nāyakena tu noditam | [kāvyālaṅkāre 1.29] iti | tatra kimucyate kathā nāyakenetareṇa vā vācyeti | anuktopālambho 'yam | etadeva siddhaṃ kathāyāmapyaniyamadarśanāt uktena nyāyenobhayathāpyadoṣāt | bhavatu vāyaṃ niyamaḥ ākhyāyikā nāyakenocyate kathā tvanyeneti | tathāpi naitāvatā ākhyāyikākathayorbhinnajātīyatvamiti paramatamabhyupagamyāpi tayorabhedamanyataḥ kathayannāha—anyo vaktetyādi | kathāyāmanyo vaktā, ākhyāyikāyāṃ svayamiti kīdṛk kiṃ nāmedaṃ tayorbhedasya vi[11b]jātīyatvasya kāraṇaṃ nimittam | naivedaṃ jātibhedasya[18] kāraṇamityarthaḥ | anyathaivaṃvidhasya bhedasya sarvatra sulabhatvāt tāvatā vijātoyatve 'tiprasaṅgaḥ syāditi bhāvaḥ | vācyaṃ hi dvayamapyetat | tat kenāpyucyatāṃ svayaṃ pareṇa[vā] yathāyogam | kimetāvatā jāterbhedaḥ syāt | arthatastvekaiva jātiriyaṃ nāmamātrāttu bhidyate | yadvakṣyati—ekā jātiḥ saṃjñādvayāṅkitā [1. 28] | evaṃ tarhīdamanayorbhedakāraṇam, yatra vaktrāparavaktrayo padyayorbhaviṣyadarthasūcakayoḥ praveśaḥ sāś‍vāsā ca yā sā ākhyāyikā | tadviparītā katheti | taduktam—vaktraṃ cāparavaktraṃ ca kālabhāvyarthaśaṃsi ca | [kāvyālaṅkāre 1. 26] iti | tathā—sāś‍vāsākhyāyikā matā | [kāvyālaṅkāre 1. 25]

na vaktrāparavaktrābhyāṃ yuktā nāś‍vāsavatyapi | saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtā ceṣṭā kathā 'pabhraṃśatā tathā || iti ||
[kāvyālaṅkāre 1. 28]

tadevaṃ tadud‌bhāvya pariharannāha—

vaktraṃ cāparavaktraṃ ca sāś‍vāsatvaṃ ca bhedakam | cihnamākhyāyikāyāścet prasaṅgena kathāsvapi || 26 ||
āryādivat praveśaḥ kiṃ na vaktrāparavaktrayoḥ | bhedaśca dṛṣṭo lambhādirāś‍vāso vāstu kiṃ tataḥ || 27 ||

vaktraṃ cāparavaktraṃ ca padyadvayaṃ sahāś‍vāsena varttate tadbhāvaḥ tattvam | taccaitat trayam ākhyāyikāyāś‍ci‍hnaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ bhedakaṃ kathāyāḥ sakāśādviśeṣakaṃ cāpyasyāsya kathāyāmabhāvāditicenmanyase, nanu yataḥ [prasaṅgena] tatra gadyādhikārāt prastāvena bhāvyarthasūcanādilakṣaṇena hetubhūtena nādhikāritayā vaktrāparavaktrayoḥ kathāsvapi ākhyāyikāvat kiṃ kasmānna praveśaḥ na prayogaḥ syādevetyarthaḥ | kiṃvat ? āryādivat | [19] āryāderiva yathāprastāvamanyasyāpi padyasya na stavādeḥ praveśādigrahaṇam, trayāṇāmapi padyatvenāviśeṣādayamapi niyamo nāstītyarthaḥ | tathāhi yadi tādṛśaḥ prastāvaḥ syāt, tadā kathāsvapi anayoḥ prabhedo na duṣyati, yathā ā[12a]ryādeḥ | ākhyāyikāyāmapi hi prasaṅgena tayoḥ praveśaḥ nādhikāritayā, [tatra] gadyādhikārāt tathā kathāyāmapi iti nedaṃ bhedakamasādhāraṇaṃ ci[ntanīyam | lambha]starhi bhedakaṃ cihnamastu kathāyāṃ tasyābhāvāt | atrāha—bhedaś‍cetyādi | lambhādirbhedo viśeṣaḥ | ādigrahaṇāt yava[?]viśrāmādivyavahāraḥ ākhyāyikāviṣayaḥ [kathāyāma]pi dṛṣṭaḥ | tataścāśvāso 'pi yadi bhavet ko nāmātra doṣaḥ | lambhādirvā bhedo bhavatu, āśvāso vā vyavahāraḥ, kiṃ tataḥ tasmād vyavahāramātrāt, kiṃjātīyatvamanayorbhavet | naivārthabhedaḥ, abhedādityarthaḥ | paricchedā hi tatra sampannāḥ kartavyā itīdamatra tātparyam, vipannānāṃ heyatvāt | te ca lambhādivyapadeśyā vā bhavantu, āśvāsavyavahāryā veti svātantryamatra kaveḥ, viśeṣābhāvāt |

nanu bhāmahakṛto niṣedho 'sti |na vaktrāparavaktrābhyāṃ yukto nāśvāsavatyapi | [kāvyālaṅkāre 1. 28] katheti |

nanu daṇḍikṛto vidhirasti, lambhādirvāśvāso vā bhavatviti | tadapramāṇamiti cet | bhāmahakṛto niṣedhaḥ pramāṇamiti kośapānamatra karaṇīyaṃ syāt | dvayorapi śāstrakāratvāt prāmāṇyam, na vā kasyāpi | matabhedastatra bhavatviti cet ? astu tatkimasthānābhiniveśaḥ kriyate | yuktipuraskṛtaṃ tu daṇḍimataṃ dṛśyata iti ||

tatkathākhyāyiketyekā jātiḥ saṃjñādvayāṅkitā | atraivāntarbhaviṣyanti śeṣāścākhyānajātayaḥ || 28 ||

yata evaṃ nirūpyamāṇo nānayoḥ kaścijjātibhedo labhyate anyatra saṃjñābhedāt, tatastāvadekā jātiriyaṃ gadyajātiḥ | ākhyāyikeyaṃ katheyamiti anena saṃjñādvayena dvābhyāṃ nāmabhyāma[12b]ṅkitā lakṣitā vyavaharaṇīyā | na ca nāmabhedamātrakena jātibheda eva sarvathā syāt | brāhmaṇakṣatriyādibhede 'pi manuṣyatvātteṣām | kriyābhedo 'tra[20] saṃjñābhedanimittamiti cet—kiṃ vai sarvā naimittikī saṃjñā, yādṛcchikyapi hi sā dṛśyate, maṇḍapādivat | nimittaṃ vā kiṃcinmṛgyatāṃ yadi tena vinā dauḥsthyam | nanvapare 'pi gadyaprabhedā dṛśyante, kiṃ te noktā iti cedāha—atraivetyādi | śeṣāṃ ākhyānaparyāyā ye sambhavanti ākhyānajātayaḥ, ākhyānakaprabhedāḥ tā atraivānayoreva kathākhyāyikayorantarbhaviṣyanti gadyajātitvenābhedāt lakṣaṇataḥ | cakāraḥ [an]uktasamuccaye | tasmāt pṛthak tāsāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ noktam | tallakṣaṇenaiva kṛtalakṣaṇatvādityartha iti ||

ayaṃ tarhi viśeṣa ākhyāyikāyāḥ | sā hi—kanyāharaṇasaṃgrāmavipralambhodayānvitā | [kāvyālaṅkāre 1. 27] ākhyāyikā na katheti bhāmahaḥ | tatrāha—

kanyāharaṇasaṃgrāmavipralambhodayādayaḥ | sargabandhasamā eva na te vaiśeṣikā guṇāḥ || 29 ||

kanyāyā haraṇaṃ saṃgrāmastannimitto 'nyo vā, vipralambho viyogaḥ, udayo 'bhyudayaḥ ripuvijayādilakṣaṇaḥ | ādiśabdena mattatāsuratotsavādiparigrahaḥ | nanu bhāmahena tāvaduktam—kanyāharaṇasaṃgrāmavipralambhodayānvitā | iti | [kāvyālaṅkāre 1. 27] tatkimapi sūcyate | evaṃ manyate | so 'pi niyamo [nāpo]hyate, adhikadarśanāt | upalakṣaṇaṃ vā tadvacanaṃ, te 'pi guṇāḥ [a]tha na vaiśeṣikāḥ, kathāyāḥ sakāśādākhyāyikāṃ na bhedayantītyarthaḥ | viśeṣā [bhe]dāḥ [yaiḥ] kathyante ākhyāyikāyāḥ, prayojanameṣāmiti vaiśeṣikāstathā na bhavantītyarthaḥ | kiṃ kāraṇam | yataḥ sargabandhe 'pi samānāḥ | sā[dhāraṇāḥ, teṣāṃ ta]trāpi darśanāt | tad yadi [kathā](13a)yāmapi yathāprastāvaṃ bhavanti ko niṣeddhā | bhāmaha iti cet | uktamatra, kiṃ carvitacarvaṇena | dṛśyante ca kathāyāṃ līlāvatītyādikāyāmapi te 'rthāstatkathaṃ bhintsyate ākhyāyikāṃ kathāta iti ||

[21]

yatra tarhi kaverabhiprāyeṇa kathanamaṅkanaṃ kiñcid dṛśyate sā ākhyāyikā tadanyā katheti bhāmahaḥ |kaverabhiprāyakṛtairaṅkanaiḥ kaiścidaṅkitā iti | [kāvyālaṅkāre 1. 27] tadetadubhayaṃ pariharannāha—

kavibhāvakṛtaṃ cihnamanyatrāpi na duṣyati | mukhamiṣṭārthasaṃsiddhau kiṃ hi na syāt kṛtātmanām || 30 ||

kaveḥ prayokturbhāvenābhiprāyeṇa kṛtaṃ prayuktaṃ cihnamaṅkanam anyatrāpi kathāyāmapi sargabandhe 'pi vā, na kevalamākhyāyikāyām na duṣyati na doṣāya kalpate niṣedhābhāvāt |

nanu niṣiddhameva [tad] bhāmahena kathāyām, ākhyāyikāmeva kabibhāvakṛtacihnavidhānāt | uktamatra | tenāpi ca niyamo na kṛtaḥ kācidaṅkiteti vacanāt | tasmādidamapi sargabandhādisādhāraṇaṃ na samarthayati kathāta ākhyāyikāyā bhedam | kirātādau ca lakṣmyā grahaṇādikaṃ kavibhāvakṛtaṃ cihnaṃ dṛśyate, syādetat ākhyāyikāyāmiti | tadasat | yasmānmusvamiṣṭārthasaṃsiddhau kiṃ hi na syāt kṛtātmanām | kṛtaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ vyutpanna ātmā cittaṃ yeṣāṃ, kṛtātmanāṃ sudhiyām | iṣṭasyārthasya svanāmāṅkanāderanyenāpadeśena vidagdhena krameṇa kiṃ nāma mukhamupāyo na syāt | sarvameva hi teṣāmiṣṭasiddhidvārībhavati kauśalaviśeṣāt | tasmād yadīcchanti kathāyāmanyatra vā sarvatredṛśaṃ kartumupāyajñāste [ku]rvantyeva, na cet na kvacidapīti | nedamapi bhedakaṃ cihnam | tasmā[13b]detadeva sthitam—tatkathākhyāyiketyekā jātiḥ saṃjñādvayāṅkitā iti | [1.28] syādetat, ākhyāyikā saṃskṛtenaiva dṛśyate | ākhyāyikāpi bhāṣāntareṇa dṛśyate, asaṃskṛtāpekṣayeti | kiṃ na kathā | atha saṃskṛtāpekṣayā bhāṣāntareṇa [na] dṛśyate ākhyāyikā sarvasaṃskṛtā kathāpyevamiti mābhūt kathā | atha miśrāpi kathā dṛśyate nākhyāyikā | tathā amiśrā sarvasaṃskṛtā sākhyāyikā syāt, kādambaryādivat |[22] kathaṃ tarhi ākhyāyiketi vyapadiśyate iti cet | ata evaṃ saṃjñādvayāṅkitā ekā jātirityuktam | jātibhedo 'tra niṣidhyate, na saṃjñābhedaḥ | evaṃ kathāviśeṣaḥ ākhyāyikā syāt, na jātibhedaḥ | yathā kathāviśeṣāṇāṃ saṃjñābhedā yatheṣṭam | na ca bhāṣābheda—mātrādvijātīyatvam | kathānāmapi parasparavijātīyatvaprasaṅgāt etāvantaḥ syāt | kācit kathā saṃskṛtamayī | kācit prākṛtamayī | kācit apabhraṃśasvabhāvā | kācit bhūtabhāṣāmayī | kācit miśreti | yathā vācāṃ bhāṣābhede 'pi na kathātvaṃ hīyate gadyamayatvāt, prasaṅge tu padyapraveśaḥ, tathā saṃskṛtamayyā ākhyāyikāyāḥ kathātvaṃ na viruddhayate | ata evoktam | ekā jātiḥ kathājātireva yatheṣṭaṃ saṃjñā anubhavati, yathā manuṣyajātirekā kṣatriya jātisaṃjñām | bhāṣāntaramayīnāmapi kathānāṃ gadyenārthopakṣepaḥ lambhādiparicchedādau na dūṣyate niṣedhābhāvāt | bhāmahena niṣiddhamiti cet | daṇḍinā vihitamiti kiṃ na pratyeṣi | tasmāt kācit kathā [āśvāsādau] gadyākṣiptārthā, kācinna | [na]hyetāvatā ākhyāyikā kathātvaṃ nānubhavati | kathā vā ' 'khyāyikā[14a]saṃjñāmityekaiva jātiḥ saṃjñādvayāṅkiteti sūktameva ||

tadevaṃ lakṣaṇataḥ [praci]nvan kathāṃ, āśvāsādibhedaṃ ca gadyaṃ nirdiśya, tṛtīyaṃ miśrakāvye śarīramadhikṛtyāha—

miśrāṇi nāṭakādīni teṣāmanyatra vistaraḥ | gadyapadyamayī kāpi campūrityabhidhīyate || 31 ||

nāṭakamādiryeṣām prakaraṇādīnāṃ tāni nāṭakādīni kāvyānītyatra miśrāṇi gadyapadyamayāni veditavyāni iti miśravidhiḥ | nanu kathādikamapi miśraṃ tatrāpi padyapraveśāt | prasaṅgena tatra padyapraveśaḥ, nādhikāritayā | ataevoktaṃ prasaṅgena kathāsvapīti [1.26] | nāṭakādiṣūbhayamapi adhikṛtamiti nāṭakānyeva miśrāṇi | kimeṣāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ lakṣaṇaprabhedo vetyata āha—teṣāmityādi | teṣāṃ nāṭakādīnāṃ miśrāṇāṃ miśraprabandhānāmanyatra bharatakohalādau nāṭyaśāstre vistaraḥ nāndīprarocanādisvarūpanirūpaṇādirūpaḥ prapañco 'dhikṛto neha | tatastato 'sau draṣṭavyaḥ | gadyapadyaprabandhastviha vistarato 'dhikṛtaḥ | sa coktaḥ | kiṃ nāṭakādikameva miśraṃ netyāha—gadyapadyetyādi | gadyapadyayovikāraḥ gadyapadyamayī miśrā campūrityapekṣya strītvam | yadāha campūriti | campūrnāma vidyate | kāpi kācidityasākalya[m] | apiśabdo na kevalaṃ pūrvakamiti samuccinoti | ayamapi[23] miśraprakāro 'sti | yadvaccampūriti yāvat | sā ca jātakamālādamayantyādi ||

tadevaṃ śarīrabhedakṛtaṃ traividhyaṃ kāvyānāṃ parisamāpya bhāṣābhedakṛtaṃ cāturvidhyaṃ darśayannāha—

tadidaṃ vāṅmayaṃ bhūyaḥ saṃskṛtaṃ prākṛtaṃ tathā | apabhraṃśaśca miśraṃ cetyāhurāptāścaturvidham || 32 ||

yat kāvyaśarīraṃ trividhamuktaṃ tadidaṃ vāṅmayaṃ kāvyaśarīraṃ bhūyaḥ punaścatvāro vidhāḥ prakārā bhāṣāmayā yasya [14b] tat pratyekaṃ caturvidhamāhurāmananti | āptā ācāryāḥ | kathaṃ—padyaṃ kāvyaśarīraṃ saṃskṛtaṃ śuddham, prākṛtaṃ śuddham, apabhraṃśaḥ śuddhaḥ, miśraṃ ca taiḥ paiśācikena cāśuddhyadhikā tu pṛthaguktā | [yathā] paścādvakṣyati, bhūtabhāṣāmayīmityādinā | evaṃ gadyaṃ miśraṃ ca kāvyaśarīraṃ yojyam | pūrvaṃ gadyapadyābhyāṃ miśramuktamidānīṃ saṃskṛtaprākṛtāpabhraṃśaiḥ pratyekaṃ trividhaṃ śarīraṃ miśramuktāmiti miśrayorbheda iti ||

saṃskṛtādīnāṃ svarūpaṃ pratipādayannāha,

saṃskṛtaṃ nāma daivī vāganvākhyātā maharṣibhiḥ | tadbhavaṃ tatsamaṃ deśītyanekaḥ prākṛtakramaḥ || 33 ||

devānāmiyaṃ daivī vāk bhāṣā saṃskṛtamiti vijñāyate | yadyevaṃ kathamiha saṃskṛtaṃ jñātamiti cedāha—anvākhyātā maharṣibhiriti mahadbhirudāttairguṇamāhātmyāt ṛṣibhirmunibhirdeśabhāṣāvadbhiranvākhyātā anuśiṣṭā satīha saṃskṛtamiti jñātetyarthaḥ | tataścaikaprakāraṃ saṃskṛtaṃ, prākṛtaṃ tvanekaprakāram | yadāha, tadbhavamityādi | prākṛtasya kramaḥ prakāraḥ aneko bhinnaḥ kathaṃ tadbhavaṃ tasmāt saṃskṛtāt varṇānyatvena utpattiryasya tattadbhavaṃ śabdabhavamityarthaḥ | tacca mahindasindhavabahirādikaṃ yathoktaṃ harivṛddhena | tatsamam tena saṃskṛtena samaṃ tatsamam, prākṛtaśabdamapītyarthaḥ | tacca hariharakamalādikaṃ yathoktaṃ tatraiva | deśī prākṛtaṃ mahārāṣṭraprasiddham | taduktam—

marahaṭṭhādesasaṃketaehi saddehi bhaṇṇae desī iti | tacca vokkaṇakaṃ kellicirihirahirasicchādikam |
yathoktaṃ tatraiva | ityevamanena rūpeṇānekaḥ prākṛtakrama iti ||

kimatrotkṛṣṭaṃ prākṛtamityāha—

[24]
mahārāṣṭrāyāṃ bhāṣāṃ prakṛṣṭaṃ prākṛtaṃ viduḥ | sāgaraḥ sūktaratnānāṃ setubandhādi yanmayam || 34 ||

mahārāṣṭrāḥ kuntalāmuralāsakavidarbhamahivācaratravaiśyādiprabhedāḥ (?) āśrayaḥ adhiṣṭhānaṃ yasyāmtāṃ mahā[15a] rāṣṭrāśrayāṃ bhāṣāṃ vācaṃ prakṛṣṭaṃ prākṛteṣu śobhanatamaṃ prākṛtaṃ viduḥ upadiśanti bahujñāḥ | taduktam—

ūhaï a viviha bhāsā pariri (?) hiaaṃ ya mottūṇaṃ | marahaaṭhiayā a atthi gahiaṃ kaïllehi || [?]
iti | kutraitad dṛśyate iti cedāha-sāgara ityādi | setubandhaḥ pravarasenaracitaḥ | skandhakamaryaḥ ādiryasya mathanādestatsetubandhādi kāvyam yanmayaṃ yasya prākṛtasya vikāraḥ, tatprākṛtaṃ prakṛṣṭamiti prakṛtam | tatkāvyaṃ saditi praśaṃsayannāha—sāgaraḥ sūktaratnānāmiti | sūktāni śabdārthotkarṣayogāt | tānyeva prītikaratvādisādharmyeṇa ratnāni, teṣāṃ sāgara āspadam | ratnānāṃ hi sāgara āśrayaḥ, sūktānāṃ ca ratnakalpānāṃ tatkāvyamāśraya iti sāgara ukta iti | nanu prākṛtāntaramayamapi setubandhādi, tat kimucyate mahārāṣṭraprākṛtamayamiti | na cātra paṭhyate mahārāṣṭraprākṛtamayameveti | prādhānyāttat tanmayamuktam | yathā hayamayamanīkamiti tatennaśyata(?) ityevaṃparametat ||

nanu sāmānyabhāṣāpi prākṛtaprakārosti | yaduktaṃ harivṛddhena— aṇṇehi a eehi a sarisaṃ ca a hoi sāmaṇṇe iti | anyo 'stītyāha—

saurasenī ca gauḍī ca lāṭī cānyā ca tādṛśī | yāti prākṛtamityeva vyavahāreṣu sannidhim || 35 ||

sūrasenāśrayā sauraseno, gauḍāśrayā gauḍī, 8lāṭādhiṣṭhānā lāṭī | anyā ca pāñcālīmāgadhītyādikā tādṛśī tathāvidhā evaṃprakārā sāmānyabhāṣā prākṛtamityanenaiva nām‍nā nāpabhraṃśa ityanena sannidhiṃ prayogaṃ yāti | kutra, vyavahāreṣu nāṭakādiṣu | vyavahriyate [śi]kṣaṇaṃ vyavahāraḥ [tatra] pravartate ebhiriti sā ca musumuria mūacchi[15b]acchiketyādikā yathoktaṃ harivṛddhena | evaṃ kṛtvā catasraḥ prākṛ[ta]mayyo bhāṣā darśitāḥ bhavanti | taduktam— [25]

saddabhavā saddasamā desītti a tiṇṇiyā a aṇṇehi | sāmaṇṇayā aï sahi āyā aaya itarāṇi āu || iti |[?]
vistarastu tacchāstrāt ||

apabhraṃśaḥ katama ityāha—

ābhīrādigiraḥ kāvyeṣvapabhraṃśa iti smṛtāḥ | śāstre tu saṃskṛtādanyadapabhraṃśatayoditam || 36 ||

ābhīrā vāhikāḥ | ādiśabdena ḍhakkādiparigrahaḥ | teṣāṃ giro bhāṣā apabhraṃśa iti, apabhraṃśanām‍nā vyapadiśyanta iti sthitirvyavasthā | kutretyāha—kāvyeṣu gadyapadyamiśrātmakeṣu kaviprayogeṣu | apabhraṃśo 'pi prākṛtavaccaturdhā smaryate | yaduktam—

śabdabhavaṃ śabdasamaṃ deśīyaṃ sarvaśabdasāmānyam | prākṛtavadapabhraṃśaṃ jānīhi caturvidhamāhitam || iti

tridhāpyām‍nāyate | yathoktam—aparaṃ triprakāratvaṃ śāstrasthityā prākṛtamapabhraṃśaḥ paiśācikaṃ ceti ||

saṃskṛtaṃ vāṅmayaṃ katamaditi sarvaṃ darśayannāha—

saṃskṛtaṃ sargabandhādi prākṛtaṃ skandhakādi yat | osarādirapabhraṃśo nāṭakādi tu miśrakam || 37 ||

yat sargabandhādi tatsarvaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ vāṅmayaṃ veditavyam | ādiśabdena pṛthak saṃghātādiparigrahaḥ | yat skandhakādivāṅmayaṃ tatsarvaṃ prākṛtaṃ veditavyam | atrāpi ādiśabdena gāvyādyupādānaṃ setubandhādivad draṣṭavyam | 9osarādīni kāvyāni yāni tāni sarvā[ṇya]pabhraṃśo vijñāyatām | tāni valayakarambakādīni | ādiśabdena rāsakādiparigrahaḥ | nāṭakādi tu yattat miśrakaṃ saṃskṛtādibhirveditavyam | ādiśabdena bhāṇakādiparigrahaḥ ||

kathādikaṃ kathamityāha—

[26]
kathādiḥ sarvabhāṣābhiḥ saṃskṛtena ca paṭhyate | bhūtabhāṣāmayīṃ tvāhuradbhatārthāṃ bṛhatkathām || 38 ||

kathā ādiryasyākhyānakādeḥ sa kathādiḥ prabandhaḥ | sarvābhirbhāṣābhiḥ saṃskṛtaprākṛtāpabhraṃśapaiśācikā[di]bhiḥ | samuccayavikalpābhyāṃ yathāsambhavaṃ [16a]paṭhyate viracyate | saṃskṛtena ceti gatārthamapi pṛthaguktam | prādhānyakhyāpanārthaṃ na tu kevalārtham, prākṛtāderatrātipṛthagabhidhānaprasaṅgāt | yathā saṃskṛtaprākṛtāpabhraṃśākhyaṃ bhāṣātrayaṃ śuddhamapi prayuktaṃ dṛśyate, na tathā paiśācikam | bhāṣānugatameva tu dṛśyate cedāha | bhūtabhāṣāmayītyādi | bhūtabhāṣā paiśācikavāk tadvikārastanmayīṃ śuddhapaiśācikām | tuśabdo 'rthāntaravivakṣāyām | bṛhatkathāmāhuḥ kathayanti tadvidaḥ | kevalapaiśācikī bṛhatkathā dṛśyate ityarthaḥ | kiṃviśiṣṭāmityāha—adbhutārthāmiti | adbhutaḥ prakṛṣṭo nānāvidhaḥ apūrvaḥ artho 'bhidheyaṃ yasyāṃ tāmāhuriti prakṛtaṃ pradhānakathanaṃ caitat | ataevādbhutārthāmiti | na tvayameva, anyasyā api bhūtabhāṣāmayyā rat‍naprabhādikāyā darśanāt ||

yadetattrividhaṃ kāvyaśarīraṃ bhāṣābhedāccaturvidhamuktam, tadeva dvidhāviniyogabhedād darśayannāha—

lāsyacchalinaśamyādi prekṣārthamitaratpunaḥ | śravyameveti saiṣāpi dvayī gatirudāhṛtā || 39 ||

lāsyaṃ śrṛṅgārapradhānaṃ nṛttam | taduktam—

tāṇḍavamaśak‍nuvatyā narttitamāviddhakaraṇasaṃkīrṇam | priyakāriṇā priyāyā hareṇa lāsyaṃ purā sṛṣṭam || iti |

chalinaṃ [chadma]pradhānaṃ nṛttam | lasyā tālaviśeṣaprādhānyam | sā ca dakṣiṇapāṇipātalakṣaṇā | yathoktam—

savyahastanipātaśca [la]syā tālastu vāmakaḥ | karayorubhayoḥ pātaḥ sannipāta iti smṛtaḥ ||

tatpratipādakaṃ kāvyaṃ lāsyādyaktaṃ tādarthyāt | ādiśabdena ca skandhakādi-[27]parigrahaḥ | tadetat prekṣārtham | prekṣā prekṣaṇaṃ cakṣuṣā grahaṇam | tasyai idaṃ prekṣaivārthaḥ prayojanaṃ tadālambya pravṛttiryasya tat prekṣārtham | prekṣā tadarthasyābhinayapradhānatvāt prekṣaṇe viniyujyate, tatśrava[16b]ṇaṃ tu sadapi na vivakṣitam | tasmāllāsyāderitarat anyat sargabandhādi śravyameva śravaṇa eva viniyujyate, anabhineyārthatvāt, na prekṣaṇe iti | saiṣā evaṃ rūpā dvayī dvividhā gatirvyavasthā viniyogakṛtā udāhṛtā kathitā | tasya trividhasya kāvyasya na kevalaṃ caturvidhetyapi śabdaḥ | yaduktam—taiḥ śarīraṃ ca kāvyānāmalaṅkāraśca darśitaḥ [1.10] iti | tatreyatā śarīramalaṅkārādhiṣṭhānaṃ nirdiṣṭam ||

idānīmalaṅkāraṃ tasya nirdidikṣuḥ prasthānaṃ racayannāha—

astyaneko girāṃ mārgaḥ sūkṣmabhedaḥ parasparam | tatra vaidarbhagauḍīyau varṇyete prasphuṭāntarau || 40 ||

girāṃ kāvyānāṃ mārgo racanāprakāraḥ, aneko bhinno vijātīyaḥ udīcyādidigdeśabhedena asti pravarttate | kimekāntavisadṛśo 'sau, netyāha—sūkṣmabhedaḥ parasparamiti | parasparamanyo yam sūkṣmaḥ svalpaḥ bhedo 'ntaraṃ yasya sa tathā | vijātīyatve 'pi sadṛśo 'sti mārgaḥ, gogavayādivadityutsargaḥ | tasyāpavādamāha—tatretyādi | tatra tasminnanekasmin mārge vaidarbhagauḍīyau prasphuṭāntarau | vidarbhā dākṣiṇātyāḥ, ekadeśena samudāyopalakṣaṇatvāt | teṣāmayaṃ vaidarbhaḥ | gauḍāḥ paurastyāḥ teṣāmayaṃ gauḍīyaḥ | tau mārgau prasphuṭau | mahadantaraṃ bhedo 'nayoriti prasphuṭāntarau | vijātīyatve 'pi śeṣo mārgo vaidarbheṇa sadṛśaḥ, gaveva gavayaḥ | gauḍīyastu visadṛśaḥ | gaveva karabhaḥ | vyaktibhedastvekaikasyāmapyanantaḥ pratikavisthitaḥ sa iha na vivakṣitaḥ | tad vakṣyati—tad‌bhedāstu na śakyante vak‍tuṃ pratikavisthitāḥ | iti | [1.101]

yadi nāmaivaṃ tataḥ kimityāha—tataśca tāveva varṇyete vibhajyete | prasphuṭāntarayoḥ suvibhajatvāt | śeṣastu vaidarbhaprāyatvāt pṛthag nocyate |

[17a] evaṃ ca kṛtvā yaduktaṃ bhāmahena— [28]

vaidarbhamanyadastīti manyante sudhiyo 'pare | tadeva ca kila jyāyaḥ sadarthamapi nāparam ||
gauḍīyamidametattu vaidarbhamiti kiṃ pṛthak | gatānugatikanyāyānnānākhyeyamamedhasām ||
[kāvyālaṅkāre 1.31-32] iti, tad bhaṅgyā nirastam | tathāhi—kaścitkāvyaracanāprakāraḥ śabdālaṃkāralakṣaṇo dākṣiṇātyānāṃ nijo vaidarbhamārga iti vyavahriyate, yathā yānaviśeṣo dakṣiṇamārga iti | tadviparītastu paurastyānāṃ kāvyaracanāprakāro gauḍīya iti vyapadiśyate | yathā dakṣiṇamārgavilakṣaṇo yānaprakāra uttaramārga iti | tataśca vāstavīyaṃ nānātā kathamamedhasām | yā hi bhrāntikṛtā sā bhavedamedhasāṃ viparītadṛśām, yathaikasminna[pi] candramasi | iyaṃ tu sumedhasāmapi, viparītadṛśāmeva, vastubhedakṛtatvāt sū[ryā]candramasoriva | tasmāt svabhāvata eva vilakṣaṇāvetau mārgau | yadvakṣyati—iti mārgadvayaṃ bhinnaṃ tatsvarūpanirūpaṇāt | iti | [1. 101]

atha mataṃ kathaṃ tarhi paurastyeṣu vaidarbho dṛśyate padyasādhāraṇo yathā dākṣiṇātyānāmeva | dākṣiṇātyeṣu vā gauḍīya iti | tatkimetāvatā teṣāmasau nijaḥ syāt | teṣvasau dṛśyamāno 'pi na nijaḥ dakṣiṇamārgavat, yathā dākṣiṇātyānām | nahi candanaṃ deśāntare dṛśyata iti tajjameva syāt | deśāntaradṛṣṭamapi hi malayajameva tat | tathā vaidarbhaḥ paurastyeṣu kathañcit dṛśyamāno 'pi vaidarbha eva, yo dākṣiṇātyānāṃ sahajaḥ | gauḍīyo 'pi dākṣiṇātyeṣu kathañcid dṛśyate tathāpi paurastyānāmevāsau nijatvāt | tadetau kāvyaracanāprakārau mārgau prakṛtivilakṣaṇo dakṣiṇātyairgauḍaiśca vyapadiśye[17b]te | nijatvād deśabhāṣādivat vaidarbhagauḍīya iti | etāvattu syāt |

kiṃ lakṣaṇau tau ko vā 'nayoḥ 10prativiśiṣṭa iti tacca mārgadvayamidānīṃ vibhajyate | prativiśeṣe tu santaḥ pramāṇamiti vibhajannāha—

ś‍leṣaḥ prasādaḥ samatā mādhuryaṃ sukumāratā | arthavyaktirudāratvamojaḥkāntisamādhayaḥ || 41 ||
[29]

ś‍liṣṭiḥ ś‍leṣo vārthagauravam | prasattiḥ prasādaḥ prakāśārthatā | samatā padyāpekṣayā [bandhatulyato]pādānam | mādhuryaṃ śabde arthe ca rasavattā | sukumāratā aparuṣākṣarabāhulyam | arthasyābhidheyasya vyaktiḥ śabdena nyāyena vā grahaṇam | anyathā duṣprāpatvād vakṣyati—nahi pratītiḥ subhagā śabdanyāyavilaṅghinī | iti | [1.75] udāratvaṃ prakṛṣṭatā kenacidarthena sanāthatvam | ojaḥ samāsavṛttibāhulyam | kāntiḥ sarvalokamanoharatvam | samādhirbhagavatpratītyanusāriṇī gauṇārthatā |

iti vaidarbhamārgasya prāṇā daśaguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ | eṣāṃ viparyayaḥ prāyo dṛśyate gauḍavartmani || 42 ||

ityevaṃrūpā daśa guṇāḥ śabdālaṅkārasvabhāvāḥ prāṇāḥ jīvitaṃ smṛtā dṛśyanta iti yāvat | kasya vaidarbhamārgasya dākṣiṇātyakāvyapaddhateḥ sambandhinaḥ | tairhi vaidarbhamārgaḥ kāvyaśarīraṃ prāṇiti | tadabhāve tvasanneva | tataśca śabdālaṅkārabhūtaḥ ś‍leṣādidaśaguṇātmakaḥ kāvyaracanāviśeṣo dākṣiṇātyānāṃ svābhāviko vaidarbhamārga ityarthaḥ sampadyate | evaṃrūpastāvada‌vaidarbhamārgaḥ | gauḍīyaḥ kiṃrūpaḥ, tada‌‌viparītasvabhāva iti darśayannāha—eṣāmityādi | eṣāṃ ś‍leṣādīnāṃ viparyayo vipakṣo 'ś‍leṣādiḥ lakṣyate dṛśyate, kutra ? gauḍānāṃ vartmani kāvye | arthavyaktyā deḥ kasyacid guṇasya sādhāraṇatvāt prāya ityāha | bāhulyenetyarthaḥ | prāyograhaṇasaṃgṛhītaṃ sādhāraṇaguṇaṃ svayameva yathāvasaraṃ darśayiṣyati | svābhāvikasteṣāmeṣā raca[18a]nāprakāraḥ | vaidarbhastu 11kṛtrimabhāvena bhavediti bhāvaḥ ||

idānīṃ yathoddeśameṣāṃ nirdeśaṃ saviparyayaṃ sodāharaṇaṃ kurvannāha—

ś‍liṣṭamaspṛṣṭaśaithilyamalpaprāṇākṣarottaram | śithilaṃ mālatīmālā lolālikalilā yathā || 43 ||

śithilasya bhāva śaithilyaṃ bandhalāghavam | aspṛṣṭaṃ tyaktam | aspṛṣṭaṃ śaithilyaṃ [30] yena tadaspṛṣṭaśaithilyamityatra śliṣṭaṃ vidhīyate | yad dṛḍhabandhakāvyaṃ tat ś‍liṣṭaṃ ś‍leṣayogādveditavyamiti | svatantrasya dharmasyāsambhavāt dharminiṣṭhaḥ ś‍leṣo darśitaḥ prāk | tanmate vivakṣayā svaśabdenopāttaḥ | evaṃ prasādādiṣvapyanusarttavyam | ś‍leṣaviparyayaṃ darśayannāha—alpaprāṇetyādi | alpaprāṇāni vargaprathamādīni akṣarāṇi uttarāṇi bhūyāṃsi yasmin tairvottaramadhikaṃ tadanūdya śithilaṃ vidhīyate | alpaprāṇavarṇaprāyaṃ tacchithilaṃ ś‍liṣṭaviparītaṃ kāvyaṃ veditavyam iti | yathetyudāharati | yathedaṃ śithilaṃ tathānyadapyevaṃjātīyakaṃ draṣṭavyamiti yathāśabdārthaḥ | evamuttaratrāpyanugantavyam | mālatīmālā jātipuṣpastragiyaṃ lolaiḥ kusumasaurabhalolupairalibhirbhrabharaiḥ kalilā vyāptā ityarthaḥ ||

yadi śaithilyaṃ duṣṭamevaṃvidhaṃ gauḍairādṛtam, tadihāpi kenacit guṇena bhavitavyam anyathā sarvathā nirguṇaṃ kathamādriyata ityāha—

anuprāsadhiyā gauḍaistadiṣṭaṃ bandhagauravāt | vaidarbhairmālatīdāma laṃghitaṃ bhramarairiti || 44 ||

taditi śithilamiṣṭamādṛtaṃ gauḍa़airanuprāso mādhuryasaṃgṛhītaḥ śabdālaṅkārastasya tasmin buddhyā 'nuprāsaḥ śabdaraso guṇo 'stīti tairevaṃvidhamiṣṭam | śaithilyaṃ tu doṣo na dṛṣṭaḥ | anuprāsadhiyetyanena caitat kathayati | anuprāso 'pi gauḍānāmevaṃvidho yaḥ śaithilyamā[18b]vahati | pāruṣyaṃ ceti | yadvakṣyati—

ityādi bandhapāruṣyaṃ śaithilyaṃ ca niyacchati | ato naivamanuprāsaṃ dākṣiṇātyāḥ prayuñjate ||
[1.60] iti dākṣiṇātyeṣṭaṃ paścād darśayiṣyati | ś‍leṣamudāharannāha—vaidarbhaiḥ dākṣiṇātyairmālatīdāma laṃghitaṃ bhramarairiti īdṛśaṃ ś‍liṣṭa[miṣṭa]miti prakṛtam | kutaḥ ? bandhasya racanāyāgauravāt śaithilyāt kāraṇāt | arthastu pūrvaka eva | nanvatrāpi doṣo 'sti mādhuryalakṣaṇasyānuprāsasyābhāvāt | amādhuryaṃ lakṣaṇam (?) ||

prasādaḥ kīdṛśa ityāha—

prasādavat prasiddhārthamindorindīvaradyutiḥ | lakṣma lakṣmīṃ tanototi pratītisubhagaṃ vacaḥ || 45 ||
[31]

prasiddhaḥ prakāśaḥ sugamo 'rtho 'bhidheyaṃ śabdārthā yasya tattathā | natu bhāvārthaḥ, tasya svabhāvagambhīratvāt | taduktam—

kaverabhiprāyamaśabdagocaraṃ sphuratprakāśeṣu padeṣu kevalam | viśanti bhāvajñatayā kṛtaśramāḥ [prakāśayantyāśayamarthagauravam ||] [?]
iti | tataḥ prasiddhārthamanūdya prasādavatprasādaguṇayuktaṃ prasannaṃ vedivyamiti vidhīyate | kathayanneva udāharati- indoścandrasya lakṣma cihnam indīvaradyuti nīlotpalaśobhaṃ lakṣmīṃ śriyaṃ tanoti vistārayati indāveva | nīlotpalarucinā cihnena candraḥ śobhata ityarthaḥ | ityevaṃvidhaṃ vacaḥ kāvyam | pratītyā bhphaṭityarthāvagamena sutarāṃ manoharaṃ prasannamiti yāvat | bhāvārthagambhīraṃ tu yad bhavet tadapi prasannameva | śabdārthaprasatteḥ prativiśiṣṭameva ca tādṛśam | yadāha bhāraviḥ— pravarttate nākṛtapuṇyakarmaṇāṃ prasannagambhīrapadā sarasvatīti | [kirātārjunīye 14. 3]
patantaḥ padmagarbheṣu lohitāḥ sūryaraśmayaḥ | caraṇeṣu varastrīṇāṃ śobha[nte vidru]mā iva ||
ityaparamudāharaṇam ||

prasādavipa[19a]ryayamitarasmin mārge darśayannāha—

vyutpannamiti gauḍīyairnātirūḍhamapīṣyate | yathānatyarjunābjanmasadṛkṣāṅa‍ko balakṣaguḥ || 46 ||

gauḍīyaiḥ paurastyairnātirūḍhamapi atirūḍhamatyantaprasiddhārtham | tadviparītaṃ nātirūḍhamatyantāprasiddhārthamapi | na kevalamaprasiddhamityapiśabdaḥ | aprasiddhārthamiṣyata eva | yadyapi atiśayenāpya prasiddhārthaṃ gūḍha़āmidheyamaprasannataraṃ tadapīṣyate ityarthaḥ | kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ prasannaṃ parityajya aprasannamiṣyato niṣkāraṇametanna sambhāvyata iti cedāha—vyutpannamiti kṛtvā prasiddhaṃ sukaramevāyatne[nā]pūrvaśabdakalpanayā vyutpannaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ tad vyutpannamanyai retādiṣyate itīdamatra kāraṇam | yathetyudāharati | valakṣāḥ śuklā[32] gāvo raśmayo yasya sa valakṣaguścandraḥ atyarjunaṃ [ati]śuklaṃ [na] tathā 'natyarjunaṃ nīlam apsu janma yasya tadabjanma tacca nīlasannidhānānnīlotpalam | tena sadṛkṣaḥ samānaḥ [aṅa‍kaḥ] cihnaṃ yasya saḥ | tathā nīlotpalasamānacihnaścandra ityetāvatyarthe iyatī vyutpattiḥ kṛteti vyutpannā gauḍā iti ||

samatvaṃ nirdeśayannāha—

samaṃ bandheṣvaviṣamaṃ te mṛdusphuṭamadhyamāḥ | bandhā mṛdusphuṭonmiśravarṇavinyāsonayaḥ || 47 ||

bandheṣu racanāsu viṣaye yadaviṣamam samam ādimadhyānteṣu caturṇāmapi pādānāṃ sajātīyabandhatvādityanūdya tatsamaṃ kāvyaṃ jñeyamiti vidhīyate | kiyantaste bandhā yeṣvaviṣamaṃ samaṃ syāditi cedāha—ta ityādi | te bandhā mṛdusphuṭamadhyamāḥ trayaḥ sambhavanti | mṛduraśithilaḥ komalaḥ | śithilakomalasya ś‍leṣaviparyayatvāt | yathoktaṃ prāk | mṛduśrutiriti yāvat | sphuṭo 'dhimātraśrutiḥ | kruddhodyasya sukumāraviparyayatvāt | yad vakṣyati—nyakṣeṇetyādi [1. 72] [19b] unmiśro madhyamaśrutiḥ | kaḥ punareṣāṃ prabhava ityāha—mṛdvityādi | mṛdavo mṛduśrutayaḥ kakārādayaḥ yathāsambhavam | sphuṭā adhimātraśrutayaḥ ghakārādayaḥ | unmiśrā mṛdusphuṭāḥ saṃsṛṣṭā ye varṇāsteṣāṃ vinyāso racanā yoniḥ prabhavo yeṣāṃ te tathā | te ca trayaḥ mṛdumadhyo 'dhimātrabhedena pratyekaṃ tridhā sambhavanti | sa[me] tu teṣāmevā[vā]ntaro bhedaḥ syāt | maulāstraya eva bandhāḥ | tatra padyaṃ gadyaṃ dvidhā | yadyekena bandhena samāpyate tadā12 samaṃ kāvyam, vijātīyabandhakṛtavaiṣamyābhāvāt | ata evoktaṃ bandheṣvaviṣamamiti | sāmyaṃ pṛthagudāhṛtam ||

atha vijātīyabandhatvasaṅa‍karastadā viṣamaṃ kāvyaṃ jāyate vijātīyabandhakṛtavaiṣamyayogāt | tadevamudāharannāha—

kokilālāpavācālo māmeti malayānilaḥ | ucchalacchīkarācchācchanirbhpharāmbhaḥkaṇokṣitaḥ || 48 ||

kokilānāmālāpaiḥ kūjitairvācālo mukharo mṛduvasante kokilālāpasya malayānilasya ca sambhavādevamuktam | ucchalantaḥ śīkarā yeṣāṃ vikīryamāṇakaṇānāmaccha-[33]cchānāmatyantaprasannānāṃ nirbhpharāṇāṃ praśravaṇānāmambhasa udakasya kaṇaiḥ bindubhirukṣitaḥ siktaḥ śītaḥ malayānilo dakṣiṇamārutaḥ māmeti [mā]mupasarpatīti yojyam | etad‌dvaye mṛdusphuṭavijātīyavarṇasaṅa‍karād viṣamam | etadeva ca [vi]jātīyabandhapūritamarddhadvayaṃ kevalamṛdubandhaṃ kevalasphuṭabandhaṃ ca ś‍lokadvitayaṃ bhavat samodāharaṇaṃ sampadyate | tadyathā—

kokilālāpavācālo māmeti malayānilaḥ | ājñāmuddāmakāmasya kālasya kathayanniva ||
bibhartti bhrāntimudbhūto bhramarāṇāṃ prabhañjanaḥ | ucchalacchīkarācchācchanirbhpharāmbhaḥkaṇokṣitaḥ ||
[kāraṇenā][ne]naivāryeṇa daṇḍinā pṛthaṅ nodāhṛtam ||

[20a] yattarhi pāde vijātīyavattvaṃ saṃkīrṇaṃ tadaviṣamamiti kaścit manyate tanniṣedhārthaṃ pādamātreṇāpi viṣamamudāharannāha—

candanapraṇayodgandhirmando malayamārutaḥ | spardhate ruddhamaddhairyo vararāmāmukhānilaiḥ || 49 ||

candanānāṃ tarūṇāṃ praṇayaḥ paricayaḥ sādeśyāt | tatastenodgandhiḥ udgato gandho 'syeti candanaganvagarbhaḥ surabhiḥ śiśiro 'pi vā | nirastaṃ samādhiṃnirvikāratvaṃ yenopanītamanmathavikāratvāt sa mando mṛdurmalayamāruto dakṣiṇapavanaḥ | [vararāmāmukhānilai]ruttamastrīvadanaś‍vasanaiḥ saha sparddhate [tān] nigṛhṇāti surabhitayā mṛdutvena [ruddha]maddhairyatayā ca sāmyāt | sparddhāyāśca samānaviṣayatvāt tairupamīyata iti yāvat | atra tṛtīyapādena sphuṭatvena vijātīyena madhyamabandhaṃ pādatrayaṃ saṃsṛṣṭamiti viṣamamevedṛśam | etadeva sajātīyaikapādapraveśe samaṃ jāyate | tadyathā—

candanapraṇayodgandhirmando malayamārutaḥ | spardhate manmathakṣībavararāmāmukhānilaiḥ || iti |

tadetad gauḍīyaṃ nigamayannāha—

ityanālocya vaiṣamyamarthālaṅa‍kāraḍambarau | avekṣamāṇā vavṛte paurastyā kāvyapaddhatiḥ || 50 ||
[34]

itīdṛśaṃ vaiṣamyamasāmyaṃ vijātīyabandhasaṃkaralakṣaṇam anālocya adṛṣṭvāasvīkṛtyeti yāvat | kāvyapaddhatiḥ kāvyaracanā vavṛte pravarttate | kālasyehānantatvādadyāpi pravṛtteḥ | katamā paurastyā | puraḥ śabdena pūrvasyāṃ diśi deśe vā vyavasthito jana uktaḥ | tasmāttatra bhavā [paurastyā] | gauḍīyeti yāvat | bandhaviṣamamevaṃvidhaṃ kāvyaṃ gauḍa़āḥ kurvanti | na dākṣiṇātyā ityarthaḥ | kastarhitvayā kāvyapakṣaḥ svīkṛto yena kāvyapaddhatiriti yaducyata iti cedāha—arthālaṅa‍kāro jātyādi[20b]lakṣaṇaḥ ḍambaro 'kṣaraḍambaraḥ | 'gauḍeṣvakṣaraḍambara' iti | tāvubhau [avekṣa]māṇā svīkurvatī vavṛte iti prakṛtam | dvayametat gauḍavartmani dṛśyate | śabdālaṅa‍kārastu bandhasāmyalakṣaṇo nekṣata ityarthaḥ | ete ca bandhāstrayo 'pi yathāvasaraṃ viniyuktāḥ śobhāmā[ta]nvantīti dākṣiṇātyairiṣyata eva |

kecittu vyācakṣate—unmiśra ekaiko bandho dākṣiṇātyairiṣyate | na tu mṛduḥ sphuṭaśca śaithilyakṛcchrodyatvābhyāṃ duṣṭatvāditi | tadasat, mṛdubandhasyāpyaśithilasya sphuṭabandhasyāpi vā kṛcchrodyasya raghuvaṃśajātakamālādau dākṣiṇātyamahākavikāvyeṣu darśanāt | tadyathā—

tāmbūlavallīpariṇaddhapūgāsvelālatāli[ṅgi]tacandanāsu | tamālapatrāstara[ṇā]su rantuṃ kaccinmanaste malayasthalīṣu ||
[raghuvaṃśe 6. 64]
samīkṣyamāṇakṣatajaḥ kṣitīśaḥ kṣapācarairhemavapuścakāśe | sandhyābhitāmrairjalabhāranamraiḥ payodharairmerurivopagūḍhaḥ || iti |
[jātakamālāyām 8.41]

etacca daṇḍināpyatyantasaṃrādhitamiti śrūyate | api ca kiyadiha vaktuṃ śakyate | sarvameva hi vaidarbhakāvyaṃ bandhatrayātmakamupalabhyate | tadanena vyākhyānena avaidarbhaḥ prasajyeta | nacaivam | dṛṣṭavirodhāt | tadana[va]gāhitagranthakārābhiprāyasyaitat vyākhyā[na]miti pratīmaḥ | tasmāttrayo 'pi bandhā yathāvasaramiṣyante dākṣiṇātyaiḥ, bandhavai[ṣa]myameva tu tairbahu manyate |

yatpunaḥ—bandhaśaithilyadoṣastu darśitaḥ sa[rva]komala iti | [1.69] [35] yacca kṛcchrodyaṃ nyakṣeṇetyādi [1.72] tatsukumārāvasare cintitam | bandhaśaithilyakaro 'nuprāsaḥ, dīptamiti ca kṛcchrodyaṃ gauḍairbadhyate, na vaidarbhairityanyatra vā tatrārthaḥ | natvayaṃ mṛdusphuṭabandhaniṣedhaḥ | iti kiṃ kena saṃ[21a]gatam | tasmāt trayo 'pi bandhā dākṣiṇātyairiṣyante, bandhavaiṣamyaṃ tu neṣṭamiti ||

mādhuryaṃ nirdiśannāha—

madhuraṃ rasavadvāci vastunyapi rasaḥ sthitaḥ | yena mādyanti dhīmanto madhuneva madhuvratāḥ || 51 ||

yatkāvyaṃ rasavatsarasamityanūdya madhuramiti vidhīyate | kva punarasau varttate yena yuktaṃ madhuraṃ syāt | śabde 'rthe ca | prakara[ṇa]sambhavāditi darśayannāha—vācītyādi | [vāci] śabde [vastuni a]rthe ca | rasaḥ sthitaḥ tiṣṭhati | ubhayaṃ rasavat madhuramityarthaḥ | kiṃ teneti cedāha—yenetyādi | yena rasena yena rasavatā kāvyena āsvāditena hetunā mādyanti prītiviśeṣaṃ nirviśanti dhīmantaḥ kavayo rasajñāḥ | kathamityāha—madhunetyādi | madhunā kusumāsavena madhuvratā bhramarā iva | madhu vrataṃ bhojanaṃ yeṣāmiti | yathā madhunātyantaṃ prīyante madhulihaḥ tathā kavayastādṛśena kāvyenetyarthaḥ ||

na jñāyate kīdṛśo 'sau iti viśeṣeṇa darśayannāha—

yayā kayāpi śrutyā yat samānamanubhūyate | tadrūpādipadāsattiḥ sānuprāsā rasāvahā || 52 ||

yat padaṃ samānaṃ sadṛśaṃ padāntareṇānubhūyate śrūyate | kiṃ varṇāvṛtyā netyāha—yayā kayāpi śrutyeti | yena kenacit [kā]raṇena padāvayavabhūtena yathākathañcit sthānamātrāsaṃyogādikṛtasāmyena lakṣitaṃ sat tadrūpastathāvidhaḥ sadṛśapadalakṣaṇa ādiruttarottaravijātīyapadāpekṣayā yeṣāṃ padānāṃ tāni tadrūpādīni padāni tadvā rūpaṃ śabdarūpaṃ samānaṃ padamādirādiruttarottarāpekṣayā pūrvaṃ yeṣāmiti vigrahaḥ | teṣāmāsattirāsannatā yathākathañcit samānaśrutīnāṃ padānāmāsannatā rasamāvahati śrutisubhagatāmātanotīti rasāvahā bhavati | yathākathañcit samānaśrutīni padāni [21b]adūravarttīni kāvye rasavattāṃ saṃpādayanti yato madhuraṃ syāt | ayaṃ ca samānapadāsattirnāma samānaśrutirnāma vā [36] śabdarasaḥ dākṣiṇātyairatyantamiṣyate | anuprāso 'pi śabdaraso 'sti, sa kiṃ dākṣiṇātyairneṣyate | so 'pīṣyata ityāha-sānuprāseti | anuprāsasya lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyati | saha tena varttate sānuprāsā, rasāvahā [ityane]nāvadhāryate | samānaśrutereva rasāvaheti | anuprāso 'pi ca rasamāvahati | tataśca śabdaraso dvividho darśito bhavati | samānapadāsattiranuprāsaśca | anayośca na sahabhāvaniyamaḥ | yathāsambhavaṃ kvacit kāvye samānapadāsattiḥ | kvacidanuprāsaḥ | kvacidubhayām | dvayena tu rahitaṃ virasaṃ kāvyaṃ na svādyate ka vibhiritīdṛśaṃ mādhuryaṃ dvividhaṃ pratipattavyam ||

samānapadāsattimudāharannāha—

eṣa rājā yathā lakṣmīṃ prāptavān brāhmaṇapriyaḥ | tadāprabhṛti dharmasya loke 'sminnutsavo 'bhavat || 53 ||

kañcit rājānamuddiśyocyate | eṣa rājā ayaṃ nṛpaḥ yathā yataḥ prabhṛti rājyalakṣmīṃ prāptavān narādhipatāmadhigataḥ, tadā prabhṛti tata ārabhya dharmasya śrutismṛtivihitasya sanātanasya varṇāśramācāramārgasya lokayātrāyā utsavo 'bhyudayo nirviśaṅa‍kā pravṛttirabhavat | loke 'smin atra varṇāśramalakṣaṇe jagati | kutaḥ brāhmaṇapriyo yataḥ | brāhmaṇāḥ priyā asyeti | brāhmaṇapriyo hi tadvacanānuvarttī śāstravihitaṃ [dharmaṃ] pravarttayatītyarthaḥ | kvacidiha dīrghakṛtaṃ sādṛśyaṃ kvacit sthānakṛtaṃ kvacit saṃyogakṛtaṃ kvacit kathāñcidityanuva canagamyametat | ata evāha—yayā kayāpi śrutyā yatsamā[22a]namanubhūyate [1.52] iti |

namaḥ sampannakṛtyāya buddhāya jagadarthine | kandarpavibhramacchedavedhase kleśavidviṣe ||
ityaparamudāharaṇam ||

asya samānaśrutilakṣaṇasya mādhuryasya gauḍavartmani viparyayaṃ darśayannāha—

itīdaṃ nādṛtaṃ gauḍairanuprāsastu tatpriyaḥ | anuprāsādapi prāyo vaidarbhairidamīpsitam || 54 ||

itīdam evaṃbidhaṃ samānapadāsattilakṣaṇaṃ mādhuryaṃ gauḍa़airnādṛtam, na bahu manyate |[37] teṣāmidamaviditamiti yāvat | nīrasaṃ tarhi teṣāṃ kāvyamiti cedāha—anuprāsastu tatpriya iti | teṣāṃ gauḍānāṃ priyo bahumānyaḥ | viditānuprāsa[sya] tu anuprāsa eva śabdarasaḥ | dākṣiṇātyānāṃ tu samānapadāsattilakṣaṇaḥ śabdarasaḥ preyānityāha—anuprāsādapītyādi | anuprāsādapyadhikamidaṃ samānapadāsattilakṣaṇaṃ mādhuryamīpsitamiṣṭaṃ vaidarbhairdākṣiṇātyaiḥ prāyo bāhulyena tatprayogāt | tataśca anuprāso 'pi tairiṣyata ityuktaṃ bhavati | na tu tathāsau priyasteṣāṃ yathā samānapadāsattiḥ | tādṛśaṃ hi mādhuryaṃ vyāpakaṃ sarvatra sambhavāt | anuprāsastu na tathā vyāpakaḥ kvacid darśanāt | ata eva prāya idamīpsitamityuktam | śabdarasastūbhayamapi | dvayena tu hīnaṃ nīrasaṃ nāsvādyate kavibhiriti ||

kaḥ punarasāvanuprāso yo gauḍānāṃ priyaḥ? dākṣiṇātyānāṃ cetyavasaraprāptamanuprāsaṃ lakṣaṇato lakṣyataśca darśayannāha—

varṇāvṛttiranuprāsaḥ pādeṣu ca padeṣu ca | pūrvānubhavasaṃskārabodhanī yadyadūratā || 55 ||

varṇasya svaravyañjanalakṣaṇasya āvṛttiḥ punaḥpunaruccāraṇam ityanūdyānuprāso veditavya iti vighīyate | prathamastasya prathamaprayuktasyākṣarasya [22b] anu paścādāsa upakṣepaḥ prayogaḥ anuprāsaḥ | kvāsau sambhavītyāha—pādeṣvityādi | pādeṣu parvāpekṣayā padeṣu cetyetattu gadyāpekṣayā draṣṭavyam | dvayorapi kāvyatayādhikārāt | yadvakṣyati—etad gadyasya jīvitamiti | [1.80]

anuṣṭubādau bṛhati ca vṛtte gadye ca sarvatra sannikarṣato draṣṭavyaḥ yataḥ pratyāsannatayā 'nuprāso gṛhyeta | yadāha—pūrvānubhavetyādi | pūrvasya pūrvaprayuktasya varṇasya anubhavaḥ śrotreṇa grahaṇaṃ pūrvo vā pūrvaprayuktavarṇaviṣayatvāt tasya sambandhī tadanvitattvāt | pūrvānubhavenāhitaḥ saṃskāraḥ pūrvānubhavasaṃskāra iti vā madhyapadalopī samāsa eva | varṇaḥ tajjātīya iti vā ekākārasmārttavikalpajananaśaktilakṣaṇaḥ | tasya bodhanī prabodhikā svānurūpavikalpotpādanābhimukhyakāriṇī adūratā pratyāsannatā punastadvarṇānubhavasvabhāvā yadi bhavati tadā varṇāvṛttiranuprāsaḥ pādeṣu padeṣu ca sampatsyate | anyathā tathāvidhānubhavasaṃskāraprabodhābhāvāttādṛśavikalpānudayāt anuprāso na[38] syāt | tasmāt sa evāyaṃ varṇa āvṛtta iti yāvatānuprāsapratītiḥ kramate tāvadantaraṃ karttavyam | ativyavadhāne tvanuprāso na labhyate | yadvakṣyati—na tu rāmāmukhāmbhoja [1.58] ityādi | atra cānubhava eva pramāṇam, yathoktaṃ prāk ||

yathākathañcitsamānapadāsattau eva lakṣyataḥ prakāśyaṃ anuprāsamudāharannāha—

candre śaranniśottaṃse kundastabakavibhrame | indranīlanibhaṃ lakṣma sandadhātyalinaḥ śriyam || 56 ||

samānapadāsattau tu rasāvahatvaṃ prasaṅa‍genoktam | samānapadāsattirapi tu lakṣaṇa[23a]to lakṣyataśca prādhānyena prāguktā | indranīlanibham indranīlamaṇisadṛśaṃ nīlatvāt | lakṣma cihnam | alino bhramarasya śriyaṃ śobhāṃ saṃdavāti bibharti | kutra ? candrai śaṃśāṅa‍ke śaradi varṣātyaye śarado vā niśāyā rātreruttaṃse śiraśśekhare | uttaṃso mūrdhni śekhara ityabhidhānāt | kathamuttaṃsaścandro rūpyata ityāha—kundastabakavibhrameti | kundastabakasyaiva vibhramaḥ śobhā śauklyāt | yataḥ kusumasaṃdohasadṛśaścandrastataḥ śaranniśottaṃsatvena rūṣyate [tadanupāti] ca lakṣma nīlamaṇinopanīyate | atra candra kunda indra sanda itiṃ pādeṣvanuprāsaḥ ||

cāru cāndramasaṃ bhīru bimbaṃ paśyedamambare | manmano manmathaklāntaṃ nirdayaṃ kartumudyatam || 57 ||

mama manaścittaṃ manmathaklāntaṃ kāmāturaṃ nirdayamatyarthaṃ kartum | karotikriyāviśeṣaṇaṃ nirdayamiti | udyatamutthitamambare nabhasīdametat candramasa idaṃ cāndramasam aindavam bimbaṃ maṇḍalaṃ paśya bhīru priye | iti candrodayopanītāṃ svāmanaṅa‍ga[pīḍāṃ] bhaṅgyā nivedayati kaścit kāmī | bakārasya makārasahitasya, makārasya nakāreṇa saha, makārasya rephasyānyasya vā yathāsambhavamāvṛttiranuprāsaḥ pādeṣu |

līlāsmitamitālāpakomalaṃ ramaṇīmukham | upāttapāṇi saṃraktalocanaṃloka[rañjana]m ||
ityaparamudāharaṇam ||

iṣṭamanuprāsamudāharannāha—

[39]
ityanuprāsamicchanti nātidūrāntaraśrutim | na tu rāmāmukhāmbhojasadṛśaścandramā iti || 58 ||

ityevaṃrūpamanantaroktaprakāraṃ nātidūrāntaraśrutimanativiprakṛṣṭavyavadhānaśravaṇam | yāvatā pūrvānubhavasaṃskāraprabodhaḥ prabhavati tāvadantaraśrutimanuprāsamicchanti | sāmānyavacanādubhaye 'pi | [23b] nātidūramantaraṃ yasyāḥ sā śrutiryasyeti hyanyapadārthaḥ | kīdṛśaḥ punardūrāntaraśrutirneṣyata iti tamapi heyatvenodāharati—nātvityādi | rāmāṇāṃ strīṇāṃ mukhaṃ vadanamevāmbhojaṃ padmaṃ tena sadṛśaḥ samānaścandramāḥ śaśāṅa‍ka iti yojyam | atra rāmā ityayaṃ makāraḥ mukhāmbhojasadṛśaścandramā iti dūramāgamyāvṛttaḥ | tato 'yaṃ dūrāntaraśrutiranuprāso vyapadeśamātreṇa na tu grahaṇataḥ | tamīdṛśaṃ necchantyubhaye 'pi | vaidarbhā ekāntena necchanti | gauḍa़aistu tādṛśo 'pīṣyata iti vā draṣṭavyam ||

aparo 'pyanuprāsaprakāro 'sti yaḥ ś‍leṣasaukumāryādiśabdālaṅa‍kāravirodhī | taṃ gauḍa़āḥ prayuñjate na vaidarbhā iti darśayannāha—

smaraḥ kharaḥ khalaḥ kāntaḥ kāyaḥ kopaśca naḥ kṛśaḥ | cyuto māno 'dhiko rāgo moho jāto 'savo gatāḥ || 59 ||

smaraḥ kāmaḥ kharo nṛśaṃsaḥ pramāditvāt | kāntaḥ patiśca khalaḥ pratikūlavarttī vyalīkaśīlatvāt | kāyaḥ śarīram kṛśaḥ kṣīṇaḥ virahadaurbalyāt | kopaśca kāntaviṣayaḥ kṛśo nivṛttaḥ | mānaśca tadviṣayaḥ kiṃ teneti cetovaṣṭambhalakṣaṇaś‍cyato galitaḥ rāgādyabhibhūtatvāt | yadāha rāgo 'dhika iti | rāgo 'bhiṣaṅa‍gaḥ pativiṣayaḥ adhikaḥ prabalo varttate | tataśca moho mūrcchā jātaḥ pravṛttaḥ rāgapakṣatvāt | taduktam—

tīvrābhiṣaṅa‍gaprabhaveṇa vṛttiṃ mohena saṃstambhayatendriyāṇām | ajñātabhartṛvyasanā muhūrtaṃ kṛtopakāreva ratirbabhūva || iti |
[kumārasambhave 3. 73]

asavaḥ prāṇā gatā daśamī daśā jātāsmākamiti kācit virahiṇī virautītyartho yojanīyaḥ ||

[40]
ityādi bandhapāruṣyaṃ śaithilyaṃ ca niyacchati | ato naivamanuprāsaṃ dākṣiṇātyāḥ prayuñjate || 60 ||

ityādi kāvyam evaṃvidho 'nuprāso bandhasya racanāyāḥ pāruṣyaṃ yatra saukumāryaviparyayaḥ śaithilyaṃ ca ś‍leṣavipakṣaṃ cakārādvaiṣamyaṃ ca niyacchati svīkaroti yataḥ, ataḥ kāraṇāt, evamīdṛśamanuprāśaṃ na prayuñjate dākṣiṇātyā vaidarbhāḥ | gauḍāstu pra[24a]yuñjata ityarthāduktaṃ bhavati | tataścānuprāse 'pi vaidarbhagauḍīyayorasti kathañcidviśeṣa iti ||

anuprāsaviśeṣatvāttatprasaṅa‍gena yamakaṃ bhañjayannāha—

āvṛttimeva saṃghātagocarāṃ yamakaṃ viduḥ | tattu naikāntamadhuramataḥ paścād vidhāsyate || 61 ||

varṇāvṛttimeva nānyat yamakaṃ viduḥ vidanti kathayanti tajjñāḥ iti paramukhena | tadvidagdhociteyaṃ vācoyuktiriti sarvatrānusaratvenām | ko 'nayorbheda ityāha—saṃghātagocarāmiti | ayamanayorbhedaḥ | ekavarṇaviṣayāvṛttiranuprāsaḥ | anekavarṇaviṣayā tu yamakamiti | saṃghātaḥ varṇasamudāyo gocaro viṣayo yasyā iti vigraha[ḥ/?/] | tat kiṃ nocyate ityāha—tattvityādi | tattu yamakam | tuśabdo 'rthāntaravivakṣāyām | ekāntena sākalyena sarveṇa, madhuraṃ ca sarvaṃ na bhavati, prāyo gūḍha़ārthatvena aprasannatvāt | tattu madhurameva yatprasannam | samānaśrutyanuprāsayostvekāntamadhuratā sarvathā prasannatvāt | ekāntamadhuraṃ cātra prastutam | ataḥ naikāntamadhurattvāt paścād duṣkare vidhāsyate pratipādayiṣyate | prabhedato lakṣaṇatastūktameveti ||

yaduktaṃ vāci vastunyapi rasaḥ sthita [1. 51] iti tatreyatā vāci raso darśitaḥ | samprati vastuni rasaṃ vivarītumupakramate—

kāmaṃ sarvo 'pyalaṃkāro rasamarthe niṣiñcati | tathāpyagrāmyataivainaṃ bhāraṃ vahati bhūyasā || 62 ||

kāmamityabhyupagame yadi nāmetyarthaḥ | alaṅa‍kāro 'rthālaṅa‍kāraḥ jātyādiprabhedaḥ sarvo 'pi naika eva kaścit arthe vastuni rasaṃ mādhuryaṃ niṣiñcati āvahati | tathāpi evamapi iti viśeṣavivakṣāyāṃ tāṃ darśayati--agrāmyatetyādi | agrāmyatai[24b]vāsabhyataiva[41] arthasya bhūyasātyarthaṃ vyāpakatvāt enaṃ rasaniṣekalakṣaṇaṃ bhāraṃ dhuraṃ vahati dhatte nānyat | 13yadyagrāmyataiva rasastat kiṃ bhedo nocyate, sāmānyaviśeṣabhāvena bhedasambhavāt | raso hi mādhuryasāmānyam, samānaśrutyanuprāsāgrāmyatādisādhāraṇatvena [tasya] pratīteḥ | samānaśrutyādestu viśeṣāvyāvṛttitayāvagamāt | anyadapyevaṃjātīyakamunneyam | jātyādyarthālaṅkāramuktamapi kāvyamagrāmyārthamekāntamadhuramityarthaḥ ||

kīdṛśī tāvad grāmyatā yadviparyayo 'grāmyatā vasturasaḥ syāditi grāmyatāpratipakṣeṇa agrāmyatāṃ darśayitukāmaḥ grāmyatāṃ tāvadudāharati—

kanye kāmayamānaṃ māṃ na tvaṃ kāmayase katham | iti grāmyo 'yamarthātmā vairasyāyaiva kalpate || 63 ||

kanye bāle tvaṃ kāmayamānaṃ santaṃ māṃ kathaṃ kiṃ na kāmayase nābhilaṣasi | evaṃ nāma tvaṃ niṣṭhureti | ayamevaṃvidho 'rthātmā vasturūpaṃ grāmyaḥ avidagdhocitaḥ | tataśca vairasyāyaiva amādhuryārthameva kalpate sampadyate na kathamapi rasavattāyai | virasa eva tādṛśo 'rtha iti yāvat | vairasyaṃ ca na kāvyocitamiti nedṛśaṃ kavayaḥ spṛ[śa]ntītyākūtam ||

kīdṛśaṃ tarhi vasturūpamagrāmyam, yadrasāvahamityāha—

kāmaṃ kandarpacaṇḍālo mayi vāmākṣi niṣṭhuraḥ | tbayi nirmatsaro diṣṭyetyagrāmyo 'rtho rasāvahaḥ || 64 ||

vāmākṣi mañjulocane iti priyāmantraṇam | kandarpaḥ kāma eva caṇḍālaḥ akāṇḍaprahāritvāt | mayi madviṣaye niṣṭhuraḥ krūraṃ praharatītyarthaḥ | kāmaṃ yadi nāma tathāpi sānugraha evāsmākaṃ yattvayi nirmatsaraḥ nirvairaḥ sānukrośastvāṃ na bādhate | ata evāhadiṣṭyeti ānandanivedanam | ayamasmākamānando mahān yattvayi na [25a] praharati | tvatsukhenaiva sukhitā vayam | kiṃ kandarpacaṇḍālena niṣṭhureṇāpi kṛtamiti vakroktyā ātmanastadviṣayamanugata[tvaṃ] tasyāśca vaimukhyamātmani darśayatīti ayamīdṛśo 'rthaḥ agrāmyaḥ sabhyaḥ kāvyocitaḥ tataśca rasāvahaḥ ekāntamaghuraḥ | evaṃvidho vastunyagrāmyatārasaḥ pratipattavyaḥ | aparamatrodāhriyate—

[42]
nanvahaṃ praṇata eva, māninī sā bhavantamavadhīrya vartate | manmathastvamasi kiṃ na tanmathaḥ kutra vā na tava kāma ! vāmatā || iti ||

yathārtho grāmyastathā śabdo 'pi grāmyo 'sti, so 'pi varjanīya iti darśayannāha—

śabdepi grāmyatāstyeva sā sabhyetarakīrtanam | yathā yakārādipadaṃ ratyutsavanirūpaṇe || 65 ||

na kevalamarthe śabde vācake 'pi grāmyatāstveva na nāsti | kīdṛśītyāha—setyādi | sā grāmyatā sabhyetare asabhyā rathyāpuruṣāsteṣāṃ kīrtanaṃ yat kiyadasabhyasamudāhṛtaṃ vacanaṃ grāmyatā | padagatagrāmyatetyuktam | yatheti nidarśanena vyanakti—ratyutsavasya nidhuvanānandasya nirūpaṇe prakāśane karttavye yakārādipadaṃ yakāramādiryasya tacca tat padaṃ ceti vigrahaḥ | susiddhaṃ khalvetadaśiṣṭavacanam |tathāvidhaṃ sarvaṃ grāmyaṃ draṣṭavyam | nedameveti yathāśabdasyārthaḥ ||

anyaḥ śabde grāmyatāprakāro 'sti, so 'pi varjanīya iti vyutpādayannāha—

padasandhānavṛttyā vā vākyārthatvena vā punaḥ | duṣpratītikaraṃ grāmyaṃ yathā yā bhavataḥ priyā || 66 ||

padayoḥ sandhānaṃ saṅgatirānantaryaṃ tasya vṛttyā sthityā | veti samuccaye | vākyasya padasamudāyasyāsa[ttyādiyukta][25b]syārthaḥ kriyākārakaviśeṣalakṣaṇamamidheyaṃ tad‌bhāvaḥ | sa eva vākyārthatvaṃ tena vā tena ca hetunā punaraparametat | na kevalaṃ pūrvakaṃ naikaikapadārthanirūpaṇena kiṃ tu vākyārthasya vibhāvanenetyarthaḥ | duṣṭāmasabhyāṃ śabdataḥ na tu vastutaḥ, tasyaiva vastunaḥ śabdāntareṇāduṣṭatvāt pratītimavagamaṃ karotīti duṣpratītikaraṃ vākyaṃ tataśca grāmyamasabhyaṃ vidyate | yathetyudāharaṇena spaṣṭyati | yā ityasya padasya bhavata ityanena padena sandhāne sati grāmyaṃ pratīyate | yā tava priyeti padāntarasandhāne nivartate | tadīdṛśaṃ padasandhānaṃ grāmyaṃ buddhyā pariharaṇīyamiti ||

vākyārthagrāmyamupaharati—

paraṃ prahṛtya viśrāntaḥ puruṣo vīryavāniti | evamādi na śaṃsanti mārgayorubhayorapi || 67 ||
[43]

paraṃ śatruṃ prahṛtya hatvā vīryavān śūraḥ puruṣo viśrānto vyavasthita ityeko 'rthastāvadagrāmyaḥ | param atyarthaṃ prahṛtyābhihatya vīryavānupacitapradhānadhātuḥ puruṣaḥ viśrānto virataḥ patita ityaparo grāmyo vākyārthaḥ pratīyata iti vākyārthagrāmyametat | evamādīdṛśamarthagrāmyaṃ śabdagrāmyaṃ cobhayorapi vaidarbhagauḍīyayormārgayorekasminnapi na śaṃsanti nādriyante tadvida eva | tacca prāyograhaṇasaṃgṛhītam |

kasyacit sahasotthānamagre vidadhato madāt | parāghātapravṛttasya patanāyaiva jāyate ||

iti vākyārthagrāmyodāharaṇamaparamiti ||

bhaginītyādeḥ kā gatirityāha—

bhaginībha[26a]gavatyādi sarvatraivānumanyate | vibhaktamiti mādhuryamucyate sukumāratā || 68 ||

bhaginī bhagavatī subhagā durbhagetyādi sarvatraiva śāstre kāvye loke cānumanyate ādriyate | tatastādṛśamagrāmyaṃ sabhyameva | tataśca prayujyate eva kavibhiḥ ||

mādhuryaṃ nigamayannāha—vibhaktamityādi | ityanena prakāreṇa mādhuryaṃ vibhaktaṃ nirdiṣṭam | sukumāratedānīmucyate nirdiśyate tadanantaramupadiṣṭatvāditi ||

aniṣṭhurākṣaraprāyaṃ sukumāramiheṣyate | bandhaśaithilyadoṣo hi darśitaḥ sarvakomale || 69 ||

aniṣṭhurāṇi aparuṣāṇi akṣarāṇi varṇāḥ prāyāṇi bhūyāṃsi yasmiṃstathā aniṣṭhurairvākṣaraiḥ prāyaṃ samadhikaṃ kāvyamityanūdya sukumāramaparuṣamiṣyata iti vidhiḥ | niṣṭhurāṇi tu svalpānīti prāyagrahaṇena sūcitama | iheti vaidarbhamārge sarvāniṣṭhurākṣaraṃ kiṃ na sukumāramiṃṣyata iti cedāha—bandhetyādiṃ | hiryasmātsarvāṇiṃ akṣarāṇi komalāniṃ sukumārāṇi yasmiṃstattathā | sarvairevākṣaraiḥ komalaṃ tasmin kāvye bandhasya niveśanasya śaithilyaṃ lāghavaṃ tadeva doṣo vaikṛtaṃ darśita udāhṛtaḥ pūrvam | mālatīmālā lolāliṃkaliteti [1.43] | tasmādaniṣṭhurākṣaraprāyameva sukumāramiheṣyate na sarvāniṣṭhurākṣaramiti yojyama ||

[44]

sukumāratāmudāharannāha—

maṇḍalīkṛtya barhāṇi kaṇṭhairmadhuragītibhiḥ | kalāpinaḥ pranṛtyanti kāle jīmūtamālini || 70 ||

varhāṇyaṅgaruhāṇiṃ maṇḍalīkṛtya chatrākāreṇa viṃtatya madhurā manoharā gītiḥkekālakṣaṇaṃ gānaṃ yeṣāṃ taiḥ kaṇṭhairlakṣitā madhuraṃ gāyanta ityarthaḥ | kalā[26b]pino mayūrāḥ pranṛtyanti jīmūtamālini meghadhāriṇi | malamalladhāraṇe | kāle samaye prāvṛṣīti yāvat ||

prativiśiṣṭasyānekasya kāvyadharmasyābhāve 'pi saukumāryaguṇādīdṛśaṃ kāvyamupādeyamiti saukumāryaṃ varṇayannāha—

ityanūrjita evārtho nālaṅkāro 'pi tādṛśaḥ | sukumāratayaivaitadārohati satāṃ sukham || 71 ||

ityayamevaṃvidho 'rthaḥ abhidheyaśarīram | ūrjito dīptaḥ prativiśiṣṭaḥ | na tathā 'nūrjita eva norjito 'pi | alaṃkārastarhi prativiśiṣṭastenedamādeyaṃ kāvyaṃ na saukumāryaguṇāditi cedāha—nālaṃkāro 'pi tādṛśa iti | alaṃkāro 'pyatra svabhāvoktilakṣaṇaḥ tādṛśastathābhūtaḥ prativiśiṣṭo na bhavati yādṛśo '[nya]tra | sa ca vibhāvanādiḥ | na kevalamartha ityapiśabdārthaḥ | ko 'trārthasyālaṅkārasya ca bhedaḥ yenocyate 'laṃkāro 'rthaścānūrjita iti | ya evārthaḥ sa evālaṃkārā 'smin gamyate | naitadevam | artho hi dharmī, svabhāvoktiścālaṃkāro dharmaḥ pratīyata iti mahān bhedaḥ, dharmadharmibhedasya suprasiddhatvāt | anyatrāpyevaṃvidho 'tra bhedaḥ | tathāpi etadidamīdṛśaṃ kāvyaṃ sukumāratayaiva saukumāryeṇa kevalena śabdālaṃkāreṇa puraskṛtaṃ satāṃ vidagdhānāṃ mukham ānanam ārohati gocarīkaroti sukumāramityevedṛśaṃ kavibhirupādīyata iti yāvat | yadi punarartha ūjitā 'laṃkāraśca, sutarāṃ sukumāraṃ kāvyaṃ ramaṇīyamityākūtam ||

haṃsā bhramanti padmānāṃ kānane madama[27a]ntharāḥ | mañju[bhir]dhvanibhiḥ karṇaiścaraṇairvarṇavibhramaiḥ ||
ityaparamudāharaṇamiti ||

[45]

saukumāryaviparyayaṃ gauḍavartmani darśayannāha—

dīptamityaparairbhūm‍nā kṛcchrodyamapi badhyate | nyakṣeṇa kṣapitaḥ pakṣaḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ kṣaṇāditi || 72 ||

dīptamūrjitaṃ sāṭopametaditi manyamānairaparaiḥ paurastyaiḥ kṛcchrodyaṃ durvacaṃ kaṣṭoccāraṇamasukumārataramapi kāvyaṃ badhyate prayujyate na kevalasukumāramātramityapiṃśabdaḥ | bhūm‍nā prāyaḥ | tataśca sukumāramapi kiṃciduṣṇamadhunyāyena yenopayujyata iti sūcayati tadudāharati | 14nyakṣeṇa niḥśeṣeṇa kṣapitaḥ nihataḥ kṣaṇāt sapadi stokena kālenetyarthaḥ | kṣatriyāṇāṃ rājñāṃ pakṣo vargaḥ paraśurāmeṇānyena vā kenaciditi gamyate | nanvetadvivakṣitaṃ kṛcchrodyamātraṃ tūdāhṛtamiti yathā tādṛśamityarthaḥ ||

arthavyaktiṃ vyākhyātumāha—

arthavyaktiraneyatvamarthasya hariṇoddhṛtā | bhūḥ khurakṣuṇṇanāgāsṛglohitādudadheriti || 73 ||

arthasya kāvyābhidheyavastuno neyatvaṃ śabdato 'rthato vāpratītiranyathāvagamaḥ syāt | gatyantarābhāvāt | yadvakṣyati—na hi pratītiḥ sulabhā śabdanyāyavilaṃghinī | iti | [1. 75]

neyatvabhedamanūdyārthavyaktirvidhīyate | tadudāharati | harītyādi, hariṇā varāharūpadhāriṇā viṣṇunā pṛthivī bhūruddhṛtā samuttāritā udadheḥ samudrāt | kiṃviśiṣṭāt | khurairmahāvarāhasyetyarthād‌gamyate | caraṇāgraiḥ kṣuṇṇānāṃ cūṇitānāṃ nāgānāmuragāṇāmasṛjā rudhireṇa lohitādaruṇāt [27b] itīdṛśamaneyaṃ kāvyam | atra hi nāgaśoṇitaṃ śabdopāttaṃ yadupādhikamaruṇatvamarṇavasya | nyāyopāttaṃ tu |

ujjahāra khurakṣuṇṇamahoragakulākulāt | mahāvarāhaḥ pṛthivīmaruṇādarṇavāt kṣaṇamiti ||

atra yadyapi nāgarudhiramaśabdopāttaṃ yadupādhikalohitatvamudadheḥ, tathāpi khurakṣuṇṇamahoragakulākulādarṇavādaruṇādityukteḥ sāmarthyāt sphuṭaṃ nāgarudhiraṃ gamyate | [46] tathāvidhasyodadhernāgarudhirāvyabhicārāt | na hi sarvatra śābdī pratītiḥ kāvye, arthe api tasyā darśanāt | yadāha kālidāsaḥ—

mahendramāsthāya mahokṣarūpaṃ yaḥ saṃprati prāptapinākilīlaḥ | cakāra bāṇairasurāṅganānāṃ gaṇḍasthalīḥ proṣitapatralekhāḥ || iti |
